Environmental Impact Report on road Drainage Work, Section N, Ring III (Sanjintan-Ping'anpu) (For Approval)
Forward
1. General of World Bank-funded Projects
Wuhan has conducted urban communication studies with funds from the World Bank showing some
communication systems need to be built in near future. These efforts lead to the launching of Wuhan
World Bank funded urban communication projects.
Wuhan urban communication system is an integrated system including several sub projects covering
infrastructure building and technical upgrading. It can be classified into five sub systems, namely road
building, communication management and security, public communication improvement, road
maintenance and environmental protection. Environmental Impact Report on World Bank Funded Wuhan
Urban Communication Projects has been prepared and approved by 2003.
The project includes Section N, Ring III (Etouwan-Wuhan/Enshi Highway) to be built in two sections, one
is Section N, Ring III (Etouwan-Sanjintan), code RD1.1 and 11.406km long; the other is Section N, Ring IlIl
(Sanjintan-Wuhan/Enshi Highway), code RD1.2 and 3.6km long.
2. General of Ring Ill Construction
Ring III is determined as a quick ring along urban edges integrated into the network of
"3-ring-13-radiations" by the general urban planning of Wuhan, approx. 90.1km long. Section W and
Section S of Ring IlIl (Etouwan-Wangjiazui-Guanshanerlu Road) and Baishazhou Changjiang Bridge,
Bridge 5 on Han River have been completed (36.23km), Section N, Ring IlIl (Etouwan-Sanjintan, 15.13km
long), Section  E  (Ping'anpu-Baima  Grade  Separation,  10.52km  long, and  the  former
Wuhan/HuangpiHighway-Guanshanerlu Road, 7.82km long) are still under construction; Section E
(Baima Grade Separation-former Wuhan/HuangpiHighway, 10.51km long) have been preliminarily
planned; Section N (Sanjintan-Ping'anpu, 8.24km long), the last section of the Ring, is the key section to
make the Ring come into a whole.
The part from Sanjintan to Daijiashan in Section N of the Ring is basically consistent to the World Bank
funded project and the part from Daijiashan varies from the direction of the WB funded project. WB
funded project extends from Daijiashan eastward along Zhanggong dike to Wuhan/Enshi Highway by
3.6km long. While the urban planned project further extends northeastward, crosses Zhujiahe River and
Nanhu Village, Shekou Street, Huangpi District, then goes through the original river course, diverts
eastward and connects with Ping'an grade separation at Ping'an Road, Chenjiaji Street, Jiang'an District,
and the whole length of road is 8.24km.
3. Background
The change with the routing from Sanjintan to Ping'anpu makes it necessary to conduct another
environmental impact assessment on the drainage work of Section N (Sanjintan-Ping'anpu) in
accordance with THE LAW ON ENVIRONMENTAL IMPACT ASSESMENT OF THE PEOPLE'S
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                 I



Environmental Impact Report on road Drainage Work, Section N, Ring III (Sanjintan-Ping'anpu) (For Approval)
REPUBLIC OF CHINA and State Council Order No. 253 MEASURES OF THE ENVIRONMENTAL
MANAGEMENT OF CONSTRUCTION PROJECT.
Environmental impact report shall be prepared for the project as required by the Classified Directory for
Environmental Management of Construction Projects. Wuhan Foreign Capital-funded Urban Construction
Project Management Office, commissioned by Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental on
January 31, 2007, undertakes the assessment and prepares report.
We have conducted multiple site surveys, collected information, conducted environmental conditions
monitoring, mobilized public participation, collated and analyzed information collected after being
commissioned and completed Environmental Impact Report on road Drainage Work, Section N, Ring IlIl
(Sanjintan-Ping'anpu) (For Review) (hereinafter referred to as Report (For Review)) by May 26, 2007.
Panel assessment meeting on the Report (For Approval) was held by Wuhan Xincheng Environment
Consultancy Co., LTD. on May 31, 2007 and panel comments have been given, based on which, we have
revised, improved and completed Environmental Impact Report on road Drainage Work, Section N, Ring
IlIl (Sanjintan-Ping'anpu) (For Approval). It is hereby submitted to the constructor who is expected to
report it to authorities for approval.
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                   2



Environmental Impact Report on road Drainage Work, Section N, Ring IlIl (Sanjintan-Ping'anpu) (For Approval)
1. General
1.1.   Objectives
Impacts on environment during construction and operation of the project shall be predicted, measures
against pollutions and reducing impacts put forward, basis provided for the project decisions based on the
surveys on the social, economic, natural and environmental conditions of the project area and
engineering analysis to guide the environmental management during environmental protection
engineering, construction and operation so as to maximize the economic, social and environmental
benefits.
1.2.   Basis
1.2.1  Provisions
(1) Environmental Protection Law of the People's Republic of China, effective as of Dec. 26, 1989;
(2) THE LAW ON ENVIRONMENTAL IMPACT ASSESMENT OF THE PEOPLE'S REPUBLIC OF
CHINA, effective as of Sep. 1, 2003;
(3) MEASURES OF THE ENVIRONMENTAL MANAGEMENT OF CONSTRUCTION PROJECT,
effective as of Nov. 18, 1998;
(4) Law of the People's Republic of China on Prevention and Control of Water Pollution, effective as
of May 15, 1996;
(5) Rules for the Implementation of the Law of the People's Republic of China on the Prevention and
Control of Water Pollution ; effective as of Mar. 20, 2000;
(6) Law of the People's Republic of China on the Prevention and Control of Atmospheric Pollution,
effective as of Sep. 1, 2000;
(7) Law of the People's Republic of China on Prevention and Control of Pollution From
Environmental Noise, effective as of Mar. 1, 1997;
(8) Law of the People's Republic of China on the Prevention and Control of Environmental Pollution
by Solid Wastes, effective as of Apr. 1, 2005;
(9) Law of The People's Republic of China on Water and Soil Conservation, effective as of Aug. 1,
1993;
(10) Rules for the Implementation of the Law of The People's Republic of China on Water and Soil
Conservation, effective as of Aug. 1,1993;

(2) Surfacewater environment
It does not produce wastewater in operation and most wastewater comes from ground water run off
caused by rainwater. Therefore the surfacewater environment of the project areas has been generally
assessed.
(3) Acoustic environment
The project area belongs to Class 2 specified in GB3096-93 and the noise level before and after the
completion will obviously increase. In addition the demographic structure shall change much before and
after the completion. For these the acoustic environment has been classified as Class II in accordance
with HJ/T2.4-1995 Technical guidelines for environmental impact assessment acoustic environment.

The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
2. Engineering Analysis
2.1 General
2.1.1 Project Title & Construction Nature
The project is called as road drainage work of Section N, Ring IlIl (Sanjintan-Ping'anpu) and is to be
newly built.
2.1.2 Geological Location & Routing
It is one part of the Section N of Ring IlIl and goes through Jiang'an District and Huangpi District of
Wuhan, in which Section K2+590-K6+840 is located in the later.
It starts from Sanjin grade separation, goes along Shunfu River and through Huangxiaohe Road,
extends northeastward along Houhu Lake residential quarter and north side of Huangpu New Town
quarter to Daishan Village, goes through Zhujiahe River, the downstream of Fuhe River, Nanhu Village,
Nanhu Primary School and the original watercourse of Fushe River at Shekou Town of Huangpi, diverts
slightly eastward, goes down through Beijing-Guangzhou Railway, diverts southward in the middle of
Guanggan Village and Zhangjiadun Village and finally connects with Ping'an grade separation at
Ping'anpu Road.

2.1.3 Construction Scale
It extends by 8243.3m and restriction line widens 50m.
Within the project full length there are no existing roads, another 886.45mu land shall be permanently
occupied including 350.77m arable land, 222.51mu construction land and 313.28mu water area,
excluding farmland.
Total investment is expected to be RMB 544 million (excluding resettlement and land requisition cost)
including RMB 548 million for road engineering and RMB 6 million for drainage works.

It includes road works, drainage works (including road surface rainwater collection and connection of
drainage works along the line, excluding wastewater pipe system) and dismantling within the restriction
lines. Dismantling and resettlement is to be assessed in Chapter Land Requisition & Resettlement. See

2.1.5 Design Specification
According to Wuhan General Urban Planning (1996-2020) Ring IlIl shall be a quick and closed urban
road with 80km/h speed allowing no passing by agricultural purposed vehicles, non-motorised vehicles,
pedastrains and animals and motor vehicles go in through inter-connected grade separations.
See Table 2-2 for design specifications.
Table 2-2 Design Specification
Items                                 Specifications
Road Grade  Quick urban road
Major line and grade separation ramps apply Class I Highway, driving spanning
Design Load   bridge cross major lines apply Class II Highway, crowd load 5KN/m2.
Design Speed  Major line: 80km/h; ramps: 30-40km/h.
Lanes     Two-way 6-lane design, 2 driving lanes and 1 passing lane along 1 way;
Each lane is 3.75m wide, Each ramp and acceletrating/decelrating lane is 3.5m wide.
Clearance Height Clerance height (spanning or through) of grade separation is no less than 5.0m;
IClerance height of roads (spanning or through) Ring IlIl is no less than 4.5m.
2.2 Road & Drainage Conditions Along the Line
2.2.1 Road Conditions
It starts from Sanjintan grade separation, goes through Huangxiaohe Road, extends along Houhu Lake
Residential Quarter and north of Huangpu New Town quarter to Ping'anpu grade separation where it
connects with Tianxingzhou Changjiang Bridge and integrates into the east of the Ring. It connects
Sanjintan grade separation on west and Ping'anpu grade separation on east, 8.24km long in total
(excluding the two separations).
The section from Sanjintan to Hanhuang Road (approx. 2.0km) is located at Houhu Lake and is
dominated by vegetable plots and non-purposed plots and dotted with some villages and canals, in
which Huangxiaohe canal and Jianshe canals tranverse the planned road. It is flat along the section
with a 19.5-21.0m ground elevation (Yellow Sea System, similar hereinafter). Several high-voltage
transmission lines from Daijiashan Transformer Station traverse the line with a 7.Om clearance height.
Daishan Village (approx. 300m) has a high topography (max. 34.0m) and heavily dwelled. Hanhuang
Road is one part of Wuhan-Huangpi Highway (318 National Highway) and 9m wide.
The part from Hanhuang Road to Ping'anpu is located in Huangpu New Town (approx. 6.24km) and
currently dominated by vegetable plots where Zhujiahe River and Fushe River original watercourse with
100-1 90m width traverse the line. 220KV transmission lines passageway stands along the north side of
the line. The road intersects with Beijing-Guangzhou Railway in the middle part (rail top elevation
29.39m). It is flat along the section with a 19.5-23.5m ground elevation. The linking piers of the two
railways under construction have been partially completed. The pier span is 33.0m and sized by
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                 15



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
2.5mx5.0m. One of the line intersects with the planned road vertically and the other intersects with the
planned road by 310.
2.2.2 Drainage Conditions
Section N of the Ring is the quick trunk line at the outsider of Hankou urban area and Chenjiaji area,
connecting Zhanggong dike on north, traversed by Huangxiaohe canal, Jianshe canal and Zhujiahe
River which are connected to Jinyintan canal, Daijiashan canal and other canals on south.
Daishan Village and Nanhu Village along the line are dwelled and the rest sections along the line are
dominated by fish ponds, farmlands, vegetable plots and canals. Drainage around is done through
existing ditches and farmlands and vegetable plots are irrigated and drained through channel systems.
The drainage system is divided into two parts by Zhanggong dike, namely Huangxiaohe drainage
system at Houhu Lake on the west and Zhujiahe River drainage system on the east. Huangxiaohe
system includes high system from Jianshe canal to Houhu Lake pumping station (Q=37m3/s, starting
level for drainage 18.15m) and low systems and low system from Huangxiaohe River to Houhu Lake
Phase Ill pumping station (Q=97.5m3/s, starting level for drainage 15.85m). Drainage in Chenjiaji area
on east of Zhanggong dike is done by pumping stations, i.e. Beidi pumping station (Q=9m3/s), Laobei
pumping station ( Q=lm3/s), Ping'an pumping station ( Q=3m3/s) and several agricultural purposed
stations.
2.3 Road design
2.3.1  Plane design
Road design shall be made in line with urban thruway technical standards according to general
planning of Wuhan Ring IlIl and pertinent road planning regulations.
The road starts from Sanjintan Grade separation, crosses Huangxiaohe River and Jianshe Canal,
passes along north side of Daijiashan transformer substation, intercrosses in turn with Zhujiahe River,
underline of Jianshe Avenue, Shanghai-Chengdu Express Railway within planning, the original
watercourse of She River, Beijing-Guangzhou Railway and east and west railways under construction
along north side of Huangpu New Town within planning, and finally reaches the destination Ping'anpu
grade separation.
Central reserve around the places from road starting point to underline of Jianshe Avennue shall be 3m
wide as the main line of Sanjintan Grade separation; while the central reserve around the place from
east Liaison Line of Beijing-Guangzhou Railway to the destination shall be 2m wide as Ping'an Grade
separation. Considering the design requirement of railway Liaison Line pier, intermediate central
reserve shall be 5m wide.
With the consideration of Zhuyeshan Trade City at Houhu New Town and Ring III for the traffic at
Huangpu New Town within planning, set up Right Entry and Right Exit road junction at the interjunction
of Ring IlIl and Jianshequ Road and Xingchen Avenue. In order to meet the traffic requirement of Ring
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                  16



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
IlIl of Huangpi Shekou Economic Developing Zone, build Daijiashan Grade separation at the
interjunction of Ring III and Xinhanguang Road within planning. Because Jiefagn Avenue is an arterial
road and a key exit road amongst Wuhan framework road network, build Nanhu grade separation at the
interjunction of underline of Jiefang Avenue and this road for fast traffic.
The road passes: Sanjintan, Huangxiaohe River, Jianshe Canal, Daijiashan Transformer Substation,
Daishan Village, Zhujiahe River, Nanhu Village, original watercourse of She River, Beijing-Guangzhou
Railway and Ping'anpu.
From the starting point to grade separation of Nanhu Village, the line shall be parallel with a row of high
voltage corridor and shall be north forward to the full to increase the land used for construction of
Huangpu New Town. The planning proposal shall apply for the line and no alternative proposals have
been prepared. Curve radius of the minimum circle is 1500m.
2.3.2 Vertical section design
(1) Design principles
0 The pipeline shall be consistent with the requirement of depth of covering, road drainage and river
navigation;
®) Minimum slope shall be used for the need of road drainage;
(T Flat vertical alignment shall be proper;
T Road line shall be agreed to current terrain, giving attention to periphery land use; the excavation
and earthed embankment shall be as less as possible for cost reduction.
(2) Conceptual design
Except Danshai Village equipped with high geographic features (within red line perimeter, the highest
place is 35.Om high), all the other areas along the road are even, where the surface elevation is about
20.0--23.0m.
The starting point is connected with Sanjintan grade separation main part. The road strides over
Huangxiaohe River and Jianshe canal in the form of bridge. Clearance blow the bridge shall be
accessible for pedestrians to walk through Huangxiaohe River bank; limited by the planed elevation of
Right Entry and Right Exit road junction of Jianshe Canal and clearance height of high voltage wire at
Daijiashan Transformer Substation, road shall pass north side of the substation in the form of subgrade;
then the road goes into Daijiashan highland whilst passes cross old Wuhan-Huangpi Highway and new
Wuhan-Huangpi Highway within planning; owing that riverbed elevation of Zhujia Rive is 12.0m,
embankment will be rather high if taken as subgrade. Therefore, riverbed is demanded to be treated
and the settlement later will be hard to control. The road section from Danjiashan, Zhujiahe River to
Nanhu grade separation shall be built as subgrade; considering the clearance height at the passage
passed by the road, down transverse Jiefang Avenue and Shanghai-Chengdu Express Railway within
planning; after the west connecting line of Beijing-Guangzhou Railway, down transverse
Beijing-Guangzhou Railway in the form of passage; connect road line to Ping'anpu Grade separation
after it passes east connecting line of Beijing-Guangzhou Railway.

The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
2.3.3 Transect design
This project is mainly constructed in the form of subgrade. The embankment shall be 1.5-3.Om
higher than current road surface. The section cross river or canal shall be built into bridge. Reduce
elevation to minimize workload provided that river clearance along Huangxiaohe River and Zhujia
Canal is acceptable.
(1) Standard Road Transect
Red road main part is 50m wide; Standard Transect shall be: 50m=3.Om (central greening belt reverse)
+ 2x0.5m (curb area)+2x1 1.25m (carriage way) + 2x2.5m (hard shoulder) + 2x0.75m (earth shoulder)
+ 2x8.5m (side slope, side ditch and central greening belt reverse). Standard Transect is shown in F
2-2.

2.3.4 Vertical section planning
(1) Design principle
According to geomorphic features of the areas along north Ring l1l, determine design principle of
transect:
O Earthwork load shall be as less as possible;
(© Meet the requirement of surface drainage and subgrade drainage;
® Meet the requirement of urban road clearance;
(A) Maintain the standard of Wuhan-Huangpi Highway for the need of flood control.
(2) Vertical section planning along the line
In order to reduce earthwork load, fill current surface 1.5-3.0m high as the reference mark of the
vertical section of Ring Ill. Increase or decrease the altitude at the places of grade separation, bridge or
culvert. The elevation along the line is planned to be 21.31-28.0m, and road vertical slope shall be
0.2%-2.5%. If the vertical slope is less than 0.3%, note the adjusted slope to ensure surface drainage
in construction drawings.
According to the spatial arrangement of Huangpu New Town, two sides of Ring Ill shall be reserved for
far future greening. Build down-transverse (or overpass) passages as access road for the residents for
the moment. North part of the passage shall be connected to the dwelling places, while the south part
shall be linked to the urban road. Slope of passage shall be controlled within 5%.

2.4 Subgrade work
2.4.1 Subgrade construction plan
(1) Road main part
The subgrade shall be constructed in step owing to long road line and diversified geographic features.
(D Within K3+150-K3+580 road section, the road is designed to be 50m wide, and average mound
shall be 3.0m. The geologic condition along the line is unsatisfied that miscellaneous fill, plain fill, soft
clay soil, silt and sludge soil are distributed within 16m scope from the surface. Ground water below the
site mainly is composed of perched water which exists in upper miscellaneous fill and plain fill.
Because of thick soft soil of large compressibility, deep subgrade shall be constructed to make sure that
future settlement is within design standard. Two schemes can be considered to use: LCG pile method
can be used in case of short construction period; otherwise vacuum surcharge preloading method can
be used.
( Within KO+OOO-K1+249.33, K2+788.3-K3+150, K3+580-K4+020, K5+500-K8+237.149 road sections,
the road shall be 50m wide and average mound shall be 2.2m. Most areas along the line are vegetable
plot. Within 12m range from the surface there are miscellaneous fill, plain fill, cohesionless soil of good
physical mechanic property and clay soil. In some areas, there are also silt and sludge soil which are no
more than 3.Om thick. Ground water below the site mainly is composed of perched water which exists in
upper miscellaneous fill and plain fill. Recommend to apply desilting cushion method.
(2) Nanhu Village grade separation
0) Within K4+690-K5+125-K5+500 road sections, the road shall be 50m wide and average mound
shall be 3.0m. The geologic condition along the line is unsatisfied that miscellaneous fill, plain fill, soft
clay soil, silt and sludge soil are distributed within 1 Om scope from the surface. Ground water below the
site mainly is composed of perched water which exists in upper miscellaneous fill and plain fill.
Because of thick soft soil of large compressibility, deep subgrade shall be constructed to make sure that
future settlement is within design standard. Two schemes can be considered to use: LCG pile method
can be used in case of short construction period; otherwise vacuum surcharge preloading method can
be used.
(® Within K4+020-K4+690, K5+125-K5+500 road sections, the road shall be 50m wide and average
mound shall be 2.2m high. Within 12m range from the surface there are miscellaneous fill, plain fill,
cohesionless soil of good physical mechanic property and clay soil. In some areas, there are also silt
and sludge soil which are no more than 3.Om thick. Ground water below the site mainly is composed of
perched water which exists in upper miscellaneous fill and plain fill. Recommend to apply desilting
cushion method.

2.5 Design Plan of Drainage work
The drainage work designing scope, including connection of road drainage and drainage of alongside
lines but excluding new sewage lines, shall conform to the length of roads based on design.
(1) Rain Water Side Ditch Project
Side ditch with BH=0.5mx (0.5-1.49m) -BH=1.5mx (1.0-1.21m) shall be set on sides of road to
collect rain water of The Third Ring Road, and drain water to the ditch nearby, but shall not set on the
side of current open ditch (which shall be used as planned drainage passage). During construction,
connect appropriately based on the conditions of nearby drainage ditch to ensure smooth of drainage
ditch and drainage safety of rain water on the road.
(2) Side Ditch of Rain Water and Crossing-street Pipe Culvert
Centerline of rain water side ditch shall be 3 meters away from on the road slops.
14 crossing-street box culverts with d5OOmm-BH=6.Omx3.Om shall be set on the alongside lines to
maintain connections of current ditches, and collect rain water of The Third Ring Road based on
conditions of local drainage system and programming road network.
(3) Pump Station
A. Passage Drainage
6 under crossing roads of The Third Ring Road shall be set, including 4 traffic roads, 1 roads under
programming crossing bridge, and 1 temporary tractor road with pile number of K2+834.883,
K3+447.883, K3+977.225, K7+977.848, K6+005 respectively. Rainwater on these 6 roads can not be
drained automatically, so underground pump station shall be set on the lowest point of the road to drain
rainwater of road to the nearby drainage open ditch or other rainwater drainage system to FUHE
RIVER.
B. Lift Pump Station for Passage Drainage
Drainage area of 6 pump stations mentioned above shall be approx. 0.6 hectare, so flow of the 6 pump
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                 25



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
station shall be 0.3m3/s on average and 3 submerged drainage pumps with each set flow of 0.1m3/s
and lift of 7.0 m shall be set on each pump station, based on design scale of the maximum pump
station.
2.6 Construction Schedule
2.6.1 Construction Sequence
(1) Coordination with Comprehensive Improvement Project of Fuhe River Outlet Section
Based on comprehensive improvement project of Fuhe River Outlet Section, construction period shall
be 3 years from November 2005 to October 2008.
Section N of The Third Ring Road of this project shall commence from August 2007 and complete in
October 2008, where commencing date shall be behind comprehensive improvement project of Fuhe
River Routlet section, but completing time shall be synchronized with this project. So integrate earth
work required in project construction and backfill of discarding earth work with this project construction,
to decrease land occupation and effect of environment.
(2) Construction Timing
Construction of Xinhe River Dike and improvement of Zhujiahe River will be the premise and safeguard
for municipal infrastructural construction and development of Huangpu New Town, according to "Spatial
Plan Layout of Huangpu New Town". Construct Xinhe River dike and revitalize Zhujiahe River to
safeguard Huangpu New Town and The Third Ring Road from flood, early roadbed shall be filled with
earth to meet construction requirements and in consideration of road foundation.
Before Xinhe River dike and Fuhe River Dike are completed, assure section from Sanjintan to
Wuhan-Huangpi Highway Section (about 1.64km) can be completed according to the plan. After such
section is opened to the traffic, Wuhan-Huangpi Highway (inside of Zhanggong Dike) shall be used as
outgoing line for Wuhan-Huangpi Highway to Ping'anpu section, Dijiao Road and Hanshi Road (width of
vehicle road shall be expanded to 16-22m) shall be improved and connected to Ping'anpu Grade
Separation to make The Third Ring Road can be opened to the traffic as soon as possible. This backup
section shall be 7.3 km long, and shall be not used as high-speed way but need traffic control.
Construction from Wuhan-Huangpi Highway grade separation to PING'ANPU on Section N of The
Third Ring Road shall be commenced, after Xinhe River dike and Fuhe River Dike is completed.
2.6.2 Construction schedule
This project shall be prepared in January 2007, commenced from August 2007 to October 2008, and
completed in December 2008.

which will facilitate the transportation of construction material.

2.1OAnalysis on Main Pollution Source and Pollutants
2.10.1 Analysis on Main Pollution Source and Pollutant during Construction
(1) Waste Gas
Waste gas produced during construction includes: A. dust (particles) produced in excavation of earth
work and storage, transportation and mixing of material during construction and B. bitumen smokes
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                   29



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
produced in bitumen paving on the road surface.
(2) Waste water
Pollution source during construction includes A. domestic waste water produced by construction staff,
where the main pollutant is CODcr, BOD5 and NH3-N. and B. production waste water produced in
operation of construction machinery, cleaning on site and excavation of ground, where main pollutant is
SS, and small volume of petroleum produced by construction machinery.
(3) Noise
Construction noise is mainly composed of operation noise produced by construction machinery
including excavator, leveler, road roller and pile driver and traffic noise generated by transportation
vehicles.

(5) Impacts on Ecological Environment
Impacts on ecological environment during construction are as follows:
A. Impacts on Terrestrial Life
Part of vegetation and agricultural land may be damaged during construction, and such vegetation and
agricultural land shall be improved after construction is completed.
Land to be occupied is approx. 886.45 mu, in which area of agricultural land and water totals 664.05
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                   30



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
mu, i.e. the roadside land is agricultural land basically, so main impacts of construction to ecological
environment lies on the loss of agricultural biomass. Meanwhile, dike on the lines need to be raised and
closed, so exists of animals on the land may be restricted in some areas.
B. Impacts on Aquatic Life
Rivers and drainage ditches connecting project mainly include Huangxiao River, Jianshe Ditch,
Daijiashan Ditch, Zhujiahe River, Sheshuigudao and Xinhe River.
Pier shall not be set on water carrying section of ditch according to design plan, when roads cross
Huangxiao River, Jianshe Ditch and Daijiashan Ditch. Sheshuigudao will be closed according to Plan of
Comprehensive Improvement Project, so piers that needs to be built in water shall only include Section
of Zhujiahe River. Construction of Pier of Zhujiahe River Bridge will increase suspended substances in
river water, bring short impacts to quality of local water and affect aquatic lives.
C. Soil Erosion
Soil erosion is mainly produced in drawing out soil, soiling and reclamation of foundation under the rain.
The project lies on flatland with many soft soil area, meanwhile dikes are adopted in the project mainly,
so large earth work load is needed to be transported from outside, and lines needs to be excavated,
with earth fill area of 488170m2, length of 6423.3m and earth work load needs to be outsourced by
360183m3
The project lies on flatland, and Mud Clearing and Filling are used in many designs of the project,
meanwhile dike is higher than ground elevation, which will cause the outsourced earth work being
360183 m3and earth work transported to the outside being 30347m3. Soil erosion may be occurred in
raining if no appropriate protection has been taken, for earth work exposes directly.
In comprehensive improvement project of Outlet section of FUHE RIVER, surplus earthwork nears to
827645m3, among which most are stored inside of north dike of CHENJIAJI, which is near to the project
and can be fully utilized. Soiling of this project shall be backfilled to that soiling site.
(6) Temporary Construction Land Occupation
Temporary land occupation is used for camps and access roads. Construction camps and access road
has not been designed now.
Now traffic conditions of the project is good, and Sanjintan Grade separation, Outlet section of Fuhe
RiverComprehensive Improvement Project, Wuhan Plaza special line and Approach Road of
Tianxinghou Bridge is being under construction, so exit roads will be employed without adding
construction access roads.
Lines will be separated by Zhujiahe River and Xinhe River into 3 sections, each section is 2-3km long
and equipped with 1 camp buildings. It is recommended to set the camp building within scope of Grade
separation Project, and no new temporary land occupation will be increased.

2.11 Comparison and selection of Routing Plan
2.11.1 Comparison and Selection of Routing Plan and Environment
The route is designed based on General planning of The Third Ring Road of Wuhan and related roads
planning data and conforms to standard of urban fast speed way.
Routing will get through the north of Houhu New Town and Huangpu New Town. Margin for route that
can be adjusted is little, because south space of the route is limited by construction land requirements
of Houhu New Town and Huangpu New Town and General planning, and the north space is limited by
High voltage electric passage that paralleled with North Zhanggong Dike, Planed Xinfuhe River Dike
and roads line. Planar plan of sections of Daijiashan Village and Chenjiaji are compared in the design.

DAIJIASHAN, turn left and get through the top of mountain, where maximum ground elevation will be
40.Om approx.. The starting pile number is KO+000 and ending pile number is K3+514.

connect the end point of Plan I. The routing will get to the foot of Daijiashan, then go straight till reach
the neighborhood of original brake gate of Daijiashan, then turn left, and then get to east of Daijiashan
to connect planning route, along with north of Huangxiao River.
In plan 11, the routing will get through the foot of south of Daijiashan. Project scale of Plan II is similar to
that of Plan 1, due to limit of longitudinal elevation of original Wuhan-Huangpi Highway and new
Wuhan-Huangpi Highway, and high elevation of route. But Plan II is unsuitable with General planning of
Houhu New City and Huangpu New City, and fails to meet requirements of boundary line control of The
Third Ring Roads. So it is recommended to adopt Plan I.

2.12Analysis on Accident risk
2.12.1 Definition of Dangerous goods
In the transportation, all combustible, explosive, corrosive, noxious, radiated goods as well as other
goods may injure personnel or damage property during transportation, handling and storage then need
for special protection are all belong to dangerous goods. The definition may cover one of the three
detailed requirements:
A. Had a certain dangerous properties such as combustible, noxious, corrosive and radiated
characteristics, i.e. substantial factors that may cause hazardous.
B. Able to form hazard, in a certain condition, may cause dangerous, goods loss or do harm to
the environment.
C. Needs special protection during transportation, handle and storage, including special packing
requirements, controlling environmental temperature, adding inhibitor, screening radiation and
erection requirements.
2.12.2 Classification of Dangerous Goods and Its Risk Features
Dangerous goods can be divided into fire or exploding hazardous goods, personnel health dangerous
goods and reaction dangerous goods according to dangerous features.
Dangerous material is dangerous substantially, but it brings risk to environment due to out induced
factors. Physical explosion is caused by changed condition or abrupt physical change. Chemical
explosion is a process releasing large amount of gas and heat, which is caused by material's
breakdown due to obtaining explosive energy. Fire hazard is the combustion of material, which requires
combusting triangle, i.e. fuel, combustion improver (oxygen) and heat (fire source). These
comprehensive external factors are the inducer that cause risk during transportation. Risk features of
Transportation means refer to Table 2-17.
Table 2-17 Risk Features of Transportation means
Transportion  Risk Type         Hazard                    Cause Analysis
means
Polluting land area       Collision or Cart Turns over
Leakage    Polluting surface water     Failure of handling equiment
Fire Hazard and                Misoperation
Road                        Explosion
transportation
Fire hazard     Property Loss                Leakage of Fuel
.         Casualties      Exists machine, high temporature, electric,
and explosion  Polluting Environment    chemical or fire source factors.
Risks may result from vehicles carrying above material after project is commissioned. Loading
combustible, noxious, corrosive and radiated dangerous vehicles will have leakage, fire hazard and
exploding accident risk. Transportation of raw material, inter-medium and product as well as storage
tank or container may have substantial hazard. So for liquid chlorine, nitric acid, sulfuric acid,
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                   38



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
methylbenzene and ammonia, special precautions shall be taken and requirements of special packing,
temperature control, radiation screening and loading must be conformed during transportation,
handling and storage.

3. Overview of natural and social environment and current status of environmental
qualityOverview of natural environment
3.1 Overview of natural environment
3.1.1 Climate and meteorology
The project lies in a transitional zone from middle subtropical zone to temperature zone, which features
clear four seasons, long frost-free period, mild climate, plenty rainfall and rich sunshine. Furthermore,
the zone is sunshine rich in warm seasons and rainfall plenty in hot seasons. For average wind
direction of this area, its static wind frequency comes as the highest over the past three years, taking up
39%. When wind blows, NE is the highest followed by ENE, NNE, N, E and W, of which N, NNE, NE
and ENE have a higher accumulated frequency of wind direction accounting for 28% as well as a larger
annual average wind speed.

3.1.2 Water system and hydrology
Surface water body along the project is mainly the Fuhe River.
Drainage system along the line is divided into two parts by Zhanggongti dike, to the west of which is an
area called Houhu where the drainage system of the Huangxiaohe River is situated, and to the east of
which is the drainage system of the Zhujiahe River. The Huangxiaohe River drainage system is divided
into two high and low sub-drainage systems. For the high drainage system, the Jianshe Canal flows
into the second-phrase pump station of Houhu Lake (Q=37m3/s,starting level for drainage:18.15m). For
the low drainage system, the Huangxiaohe River flows into the third-phrase pump station of Houhu
(Q=97.5m3/s, starting level for drainage:15.85m). For drainage of the Chenjiaji area to the east of
Zhanggong Dike, drainage pump stations are employed. They include three pump stations (Beidi,
Q=9m3/s; Laobei, Q=1m 3/s; Ping'an, Q=3m3/s) and several irrigation pump stations.
Drainage system along the line is shown in Attached Drawing 3.
For the canal section between Wolongtan and the river mouth of the Fuhe River, average gradient of its

Spacing of its dike is from 500m to 800m. Southern part of the canal is the Laohe River (also named
Zhujiahe River) extends 8.2km and appears S-shape. Its river training consists mainly of single
cross-section and its spacing of dike is from 250m to 300m. At the upper stretches of diverging point of
northern and southern parts of the canal stands Daijiashan Bridge. The old course of the Sheshui River
between large and small South Lakes is 100 to 150 meters wide and joins the Xinhe River and the
Zhujiahe River respectively.
For the lower Huge River stretches of Wolongtan, floods occur when water level of the Changjiang

3.1.3 Topography and landforms
The project is involved in two administrative districts (Huangpi and Jiang'an Districts). The area along
the line stands in the middle and lower reaches of the Changjiang River and adjacent to the east edge
of Jianghan Plain. It is the first terrace of the Changjiang River and the Fuhe Riverand a high over-bank
area of the Changjiang River. In general, its terrain is low and its surface flat. Its northwest part is a little
higher than its southeast part. With rough sparsely-scattered hills of small gradient, the area is a little
inclined to the Changjiang River. Its landform type is mainly characterized by delta plain of rivers and
lakes, which is low, flat, vast and with no large slopes and generally 21.0 to 23.0 meters above sea
level.
The line travels through the Zhujia Rive, the Sheshui River old course and Beijing-Guangzhou railway
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                  41



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
and extends west east. The area along the line has abundant surface water. The Fuhe Riversection
between Fuhe Bridge and Second Daishan Bridge flows from south west to north east. Mud layer of its
river bed is thin. There is no over-bank at its left bank, of which slops are steep. On these slops there
are nearly-ruined small hills and their surface is a little rough. Their attitude is 25.0 to 27.0m. At the right
bank of the river section is a wide over-bank area, which is 20.5 to 21.7 meters above sea level. Front
edge of the over-bank area assumes steep slop-shape. At its rear edge is a dike surrounding a flat first
terrace with an attitude of 22.1 to 22.3m. The mouth of the Sheshui River old course lies at high
over-bank areas of both the Changjiang River and the Fuhe River. The Sheshui River flows from north
to south into the Changjiang River. Mud layer of its river bed is thin. There is no over-bank at both
banks. Fifteen meters away from banks, a dike with an attitude of 26.0 to 27.Om surrounds flat farm
lands which are 22.2 to 23.6 meters above sea level.
3.1.4 Geology
Since faulted structure of base of where project construction is conducted does not grow and
contemporary structure movement mainly takes the form of vertical movement, exposed strata are
almost Silurian period and Quaternary system. Ground layer of Quaternary system covers a vast area,
taking up more than 95% of total area along the line. It is 15 to 50m in thickness and consists mainly of
impacting and lacustrine soil layers of Holocene series and upper Pleistogene of Quaternary system.
Lithology mainly includes clay, earthbound, loam, sand soil and mucky soil. Exposed rock base of
areas along the line is sparsely-scattered and composed mainly of sandstone of Silurian system and
Cretaceous-Lower Tertiary.
According to China Seismic Motion Parameters Zoning Map newly compiled by China Seismological
Bureau  (GB18306-2001) , seismic peak ground acceleration of areas along the line is 0.05g and its
cycle of reaction spectrum feature of seismic ground motion is 0.35s. Its corresponding seismic
intensity is VI degree and in general, the area remains stable.
Underground water inside the area mainly contains non-erosive carbonate. According to deposit
condition of underground water and features of water-bearing formation, underground water can be
classified into pore water in loose rocks of Quaternary system and crack water in clastic rocks. Pore
water in loose rocks can also be sub-divided into pore phreatic water and pressure-bearing water, of
which pore phreatic water lies mainly in upper sand soil layer. Since water-bearing layer possesses
such physical properties as changeable thickness, bad connectivity, and bad and uneven water-bearing
and water penetration, underground water is generally 0.5 to 1.5 meters in depth. Pore
pressure-bearing water, however, lies mainly in sand soil layer and gravel layer. Owning to its stable
distribution, good deposit condition and water penetration, it has a general depth of 8.5 to 25m. In
general, this water-bearing layer advances thinner and thinner from front edge of its terrace to rear
edge. Pore pressure-bearing water-bearing formation of sand soil layer and gravel layer not far from the
Changjiang River is directly connected to sand layer of the Changjiang River bed, leading to direct
connection of water-bearing layer and river water and thus forming close connection. During the period
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                     42



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
of flooding, the Changjiang River will replenish underground water-bearing layer with water and vice
versa.
3.2 Overview of social environment
The project cuts through two districts of Wuhan City (Huangpi and Jiang'an Districts).
3.2.1 Wuhan City
Wuhan Metropolitan is called "Han" for short and conventionally named "Jiangcheng". Lying in the
center of inland China, in the east of Hubei province and at the convergence of the Hanjiang River and
the Changjiang River, Wuhan Metropolitan is the capital of Hubei province, the economic, scientific and
technological, educational and cultural centre of Central China and middle reaches of the Changjiang
River as well as one of metropolitans and an important traffic terminal of China. It stands between East
Longitude 113°41' and 115005' and between North Latitude 29°58' and 31°22'. On plane right angle
co-ordinate, its largest distances from east to west and from south to north are 134km and i 155km
respectively. It covers an area of 8467.11 km2which accounts for 4.6% of total area of Hubei province.
The area of its city area is 222.2km2.
In 2005, Wuhan Metropolitan had thirteen administrative districts including Jiang'an, Jianghan, Qiaokou,
Hanyang, Wuchang, Qingshan, Hongshan, Caidian, Jiangxia, Huangpi, Xinzhou, Dongxihu and
Hannan Districts. These districts govern 119 sub-district offices, 19 towns and 15 sub-counties. There
are 3138 self-administration organizations of people, of which 1086 are community committees and
2052 villagers committees.
According to 1% sample survey of population conducted in 2005, there are 8.58 million residents
including fifty peoples in the city.
In 2005, economy of Wuhan Metropolitan kept growing fast and smoothly. Its annual Gross Output
Value reached 223.8 trillion Yuan RMB, of which 18.06 trillion Yuan is from agriculture. Added values of
its industrial output and construction industry were 85.2 trillion Yuan and 16.7 trillion Yuan respectively.
Its fixed asset investments and retail sales of consumer goods totaled 105.518 trillion Yuan and
112.864 trillion Yuan respectively.
3.2.2 Jiang'an District
Jiang'an district lies at the north of the Changjiang River and in the east of Hankou (one of three
administrative areas of Wuhan City). Adjacent to Huangpi District in the east and to Jiang'an District in
the west, facing Wuchang and Hongshan districts across the Changjiang River to the south and
bordering on Dongxihu District in the north, it is the seat of Wuhan Municipal Committee of the CPC and
Wuhan Municipal Government and the important political, banking, information and cultural centre.
Jiang'an District covers an area of 64.24km2 including farm lands of 346.8 hectares. Its total population
with register is 1.105 million including 23 peoples such as Han, Hui and Miao peoples. It governs 15
sub-district administrative offices, one sub-county, 159 community committees and 24 villagers
committees. Chenjiaji sub-district has an area of 8.00km2 and a population of 6417. It governs one
community committee and 4 villagers committees. Houhu sub-county has an area of 23.00km2 and a
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                43



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
population of 57500. It governs 4 community committees and 20 villagers committees.
In 2005, annual Gross Output Value of Jiang'an District reached 14 trillion Yuan. Its fixed asset
investments were 9.421 trillion Yuan. Added values of its agricultural and industrial output reached 99
million Yuan and 2.333 trillion Yuan respectively. Its retail sales of consumer goods totaled 11.643
trillion Yuan, of which 2.135 trillion Yuan was turned over to national finance.
The area of newly-increased public lawn that year was 160,200 m2 and public lawn area per person
reached 4.45m2.
Jiang'an District has jurisdiction over 51 middle schools, 10 vocational schools, 47 primary schools, 54
kindergartens, 5 cultural institutions and 385 medical institutions of all levels.
3.2.3 Huangpi District
Huangpi District lies in the north of Wuhan Metropolitan, adjacent to Hongan county and Xinzhou
district in the east, facing Jiang'an and Qiaokou districts in the south, contiguous to Xiaogan City in the
west and bordering on Dawu county in the north.
Huangpi District covers an area of 2261 km2 including farm lands of 56,700 hectares. Its total population
with register is 1.105 million including 22 peoples such as Han, Hui and Zhang peoples. It has 7
sub-district administrative offices, 2 sub-counties, 6 towns, one development zone, 2 forest farms, one
scenic spot, 43 community committees and 591 villagers committees.
In 2005, annual Gross Output Value of Huangpi District reached 8.818 trillion Yuan. Its fixed asset
investments were 2.842 trillion Yuan. Added values of its agricultural and industrial output reached
2.707 trillion Yuan and 2.142 trillion Yuan respectively. Its Gross Output Value of construction
installation totaled 2.8 trillion Yuan. Its retail sales of consumer goods totaled 4.19 trillion Yuan, of which
711 million Yuan was turned over to national finance.
The area of newly-increased public lawn that year was 14,300 m2and that of artificial forest reached
2066.7 hectares.
Huangpi District administers one second specialized school, 55 middle schools, 2 vacational schools,
268 primary schools, 40 kindergartens, 8 cultural institutions and 74 medical institutions of all levels.

Zone at the convergence of Houhu Road and Chama Road; Dijiao Industrial Zone at the west of
Hanhuang Road: At present, the building area of living communities built reaches 2962800 m2
accommodating households of 25735. Its population totals 82351. The building area of living
communities under construction reaches 1327900 m2 which will accommodate households of 11534.
Its population will total 36909.

3.3.2 Overview of improvement planning of the Fuhe River
Comprehensive improvement project of river mouth of the Fuhe River(one tributary of the Changjiang
River) includes the following aspects: (1) Expanding and deepening of Fuhe Rivermouth and clearing
flood obstacles to achieve its design flood discharge capability (2) Heightening its dike and enhancing
flood discharge requirements so as to form a protection zone surrounding Chenjiaji area of Wuhan
Metropolitan (3) Improving its water system and building its internal drainage facilities.
Construction items of this improvement project consist mainly of the following aspects: (1) Expanding
and deepening the Fuhe River10.27km along its axial line (2) Dredging the blocked section between
Daijiashan Bridge and Santong Bridge (3) Blocking the old river course of 10.4 km between Zhujiahe
River and Sheshui River (4) Improving and building big and small Nanhu dike of 6.36km (including
Wuha  M
3.3.2  Overiewpof imperovesitt f niomentapanngo lh PruhecRiver4



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
filling the dike, wave fences and pressure immersing fences; embanking; blocking seepage; building
roads at top of dike and filling ponds at low-laying land ) (5) Consolidating Xiyuanhu dike of 3.2km and
three bridges affected by expanding and deepening construction of the Xinhe River(Daijiashan bridge,
Sandao bridge and Xinhe River bridge) and (6) Installing necessary management facilities
Improvement construction items involved in the project include such aspects as dredging blocks near
Daijiashan Bridge, blocking the Zhujiahe River and the old river course of the Sheshui River and
building regional drainage facilities.
(1) Dredging blocks
Daijiashan Bridge consists of No 1 Bridge in Hankou and No 2 Bridge in Huangpi district. The two
bridges are connected with roads. At present, cofferdam at upstream stretches of No 1 Bridge has
blocked waterway of under the bridge. For the purpose of the project, removal of Daijiashan Road
Bridge is under planning. Earth dike used for connection will be replaced by an overhead section. The
bridge to be built will be 400m in length. Cofferdam of 1000m at river course and flood discharge
obstacles will be removed. For dredging, cross-section design will be employed so as to form a single
river course.
(2) Blocking the Zhujiahe River and the old river course of the Sheshui River
For blocking the Zhujiahe River and the old river course of the Sheshui River, dredging and filling
construction method will be employed. Elevation of dredging and filling construction is 22.00m. Its top
will be covered with cultivated soil of 0.5 meter thick. Zhujia Rive and old river course of Sheshui River
are 8.2km and 2.2km in length respectively. Earth and rock dam structure will be utilized for blocking.
There are three sections to be blocked. They are Zhujiahe River inlet and outlet, and inlet of old river
course of Sheshui River.
(3) Regional drainage
Diversion of the Zhujiahe River will directly affect regional drainage. New water discharge outlets and
gates will be built along the Xinhe River. Since planning of land utilization of this area is not clear yet,
function, address, scope and operating conditions of water discharge gate have yet to be determined.
Considering drainage of farm lands and residents during construction, initial pump stations for drainage
will be removed and new ones will be built in areas surrounded by the Xinjian Dike. The new pump
stations will have the same scope as that of old ones. Self-discharge gates at low water level will be
removed and blocked. New pump stations will be responsible for drainage during construction when
water level gets low.
With a view to actual conditions of comprehensive improvement project of Fuhe Rivermouth, its
construction will be completed in three years. That is, its construction will last from November 2005 to
October 2008. Its construction is now under way and the Zhujiahe River is not blocked yet.

3.4.3 Quality status of acoustic environment
(1) Standards & specifications of measurement
Measurement will be conducted according to GB/T 3222-94 Acoustics-Measuring approach of
Environmental Noise and GB/T 14623-93 Measuring approach for Environmental Noise of Urban Area.
(2) Measuring approach
(OMeasuring instrument: RION NL-31 precision sound level meter will be utilized for measuring status
of environmental noise this time. Measuring instruments (including sound source calibrator) must be
those which have passed annual metrological verification conducted by metrological administrative
department concerned before being put into use. Before and after measurement each time, these
instruments shall be calibrated by BK4231 sound source calibrator.
(ZDate and method of measurement: Status measuring of environmental noise will be conducted in the
daytime and nighttime. Typical time segments will be selected to measure 10 minutes equivalent
consecutive sound level-A. For those areas affected by large traffic noise, 20 minutes equivalent
consecutive sound level A will be measured so as to actually reflect status of their acoustic
environment.
(M)Measurement and evaluation quantity: Measurement and evaluation quantity is equivalent
consecutive sound level A.
(3) Point layout principle of points to be measured
Wuhan Environmental Protection Institute conducted survey and measurement of environmental status
sensitive areas along the line from March 26 to 29 2007. For this evaluation and measurement of
environmental noise, all sensitive areas will be covered.
The line travels through such residential areas as Daishan, Nanhu, Shuangqiao and Xinjian villages.
When the line arrives at residential areas, measured points will only be arranged at one side of the line.
There will be seven measured points to be arranged along the line. Arrangement and location of
measured points of quality status of acoustic environment are given in Table 3-7 and Attached Drawing
1.
(4) Measuring results and evaluation

indicates that quality of acoustic environment along the line is good.

3.5 Quality status of eco-environment
3.5.1 Soil environment
Owning to Pedodiversity of soil of areas along the line, their soil comes in a variety of types. Based on
regional combination law of soil and landforms, these areas lie mainly at the converging stretches of
river and lake facies sediment. Soil type includes rice soil, moisture soil, red soil and Yellow Brown Soil.
The area of rice soil tops that of others. Their main soil type is river alluvial moisture soil followed by
lake alluvial moisture soil and part of Yellow Brown Soil. The soil is rich in organic matter. Its hardness
and PH value remain mediate.
3.5.2 Biotic resources
Areas along the line are a transitional zone from middle subtropical evergreen broadleaf forests to north
subtropical broadleaf forests. According to statistics in 2003, there are Pteridophyta and seed plants of
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                    51



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
106 families in Wuhan Metropolitan. They can be further divided into 607 types and 1066 subtypes.
They possess floristic elements of plants of both south and north. Typical vegetation type of these
areas is mingled forest consisting of evergreen broadleaf forest and deciduous broadleaf forest.
Owning to prolong human activities of reclamation and cultivation, primitive vegetation of these areas
has been almost completely destroyed. Now these areas are mainly covered by artificial vegetation.
However, climate and soil quality of these areas are good. There is a rich vegetation cover along rivers
and are hardly naked fields. River-beaches are covered with plenty of weeds. The area surrounded by
the dike at the edge of river-beaches is covered mainly by farm vegetation and fish ponds.
Habitats of wildlives in areas along the line are decreasing due to destruction of natural vegetation.
There are no large vertebrates except for such common animals in farming zones and water areas as
Amphibian animals, reptiles, birds and small mammals in these areas. Wildlives in farming zones
include Paddy frog, cantor, wall lizard, Amphiesma stolata, sparrow, and turtledove and grass rabbit.
Wildlives in water areas mainly include turtle, crab, green head duck and heron.
In rivers and ponds in areas along the line grow all kinds of plankton, macro-benthic animals, aquatic
vascular plants and fish. Diatom possesses a lion share in plankton. Aquatic insects and soft animals
have a large proportion of macro-benthic animals. Hydrilla verticillata and golden hair grass are main
members of aquatic vascular plants while black carp, grass fish, silver carp and big head carp possess
a lion share of fish.
Owning to impact caused by such factors as water contamination resulting from human activities, fish
habitats have been interfered and destroyed. In general, aquatic organism resources in areas along the
line tend to be declining.
According to a survey conducted by agricultural authorities of Huangpi and Jiang'an districts, no
endangered aquatic species and wildlives and plants, which need special state protection, have been
found in areas along the line yet. There are no natural protection zones, ecological function zones,
forest parks, geological parks, scenic spots, and important historical and cultural relics, either.
3.6 Main environmental problems
Through the analysis of contents mentioned above, we can see that main environmental problems in
areas along the line lie in water quality of the Fuhe Riveras receiving water body, of which water quality
can not satisfy its function requirements. In 2005, standard indexes of total nitrogen amount and
ammonia nitrogen of the Fuhe River(the section between Huanghualao and its river mouth to the
Changjiang River) were greater than 1. That is, these indexes exceeded limited values. Average annual
individual quality index of PM10 of air environment was greater than 1. That is, it had an excellent quality
of acoustic environment.

4. Prediction, analysis and evaluation of effects upon the environment
4.1 Prediction, analysis and evaluation of construction effects upon the environment
4.1.1 Analysis of effects upon eco-environment
(1)Terrestrial animals
OTerrestrial plants
The project under planning will travel through Jiang'an and Huangpi districts of Wuhan
Metropolitan. The two districts belong to part of Jianhan Plain featuring a flat surface. Vegetation
of areas which will be affected by the project consists mainly of artificial vegetation. The areas are
dominated by agricultural vegetation along with a few bushes and shrubs. There is little primitive
vegetation and plants specially protected by the state along the line.
Picture 4-1: Main vegetation of ground surface along the line
I                                I.
D1                     ..
Figure 4-1: main vegetation type of ground surface along the line
Main construction links affecting vegetation during road construction come as follows:
*Construction of bridges, tunnels, culverts and interchanges will exert an irreversible effect on
vegetation. It will cause damage to eco-environment of vegetation and destroy growth
environment of single biological body.
*Road construction will cause damage to vegetation along the road to be built. Based on the
survey on vegetation distribution status, it is not difficult to see that vegetation type to be directly
affected by the project mainly includes farm land and shrub-grass land.
*During construction, such interim yards and roads for construction as builder's road, batching
plant, builder's yard, prefabricated plant and stacking yard will cause direct damage to eco-system
and vegetation of farm lands, thus changing structure of arthropod community and exerting a
direct effect on stabilization and diversification of arthropod community. Since the effect is
irreversible, care shall therefore be excised to avoid builder's roads cutting through stretches of
farm lands when designing these roads. More efforts shall be made to improve agricultural
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               53



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN  to PING  ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
techniques to make up output drop resulting from declining of areas of farm lands when the project
is completed.
*During construction, vegetation near construction site will be damaged due to rolling of
mechanical equipment, and trampling of construction personnel and so on..
There is stable agricultural eco-system forming over years along the line. According to a field
survey, there are no plants needing to be specially protected by the state rather than agricultural
vegetation in areas along the line. Agricultural vegetation derives from artificial cultivation. Since
project construction will destroy surface vegetation of areas along the line, losses of surface
vegetation will sure exert an effect on existing eco-system. However, destructive areas of surface
vegetation are small with respect to those areas along the line. For non-agricultural vegetation,
biomass loss can be compensated by means of road planting. In general, project construction will
not affect stability and integrity of eco-system of areas along the line. To reduce damage to
vegetation as much as possible during construction, the following measures will be taken. They
include (1) reducing building rubbish, (2) clearing redundant earth and stone promptly, and (3)
avoiding trampling and rolling vegetation on site. Furthermore, such measures as protecting road
side slope, planting trees and grass will be taken so as to restore part of destroyed vegetation
naturally and artificially.
(9) Terrestrial animals
* Effects upon Amphibians
This kind of animals inhabits in rivers, slopes, water ponds and drainage ditches in areas along the
line. Since infrastructure construction related to the project will sure result in change of water
quality and ecological environment near water areas, the habitats of these amphibian animals will
also change and these animals will get fewer and fewer.
* Effects upon reptiles and small animals
Reptiles such as lizards and snakes in areas along the line will be forced to migrate farther
because their habitats are damaged by project construction. But this phenomenon will only
happen in those areas near construction field and their habitats will, in general, not be affected.
Population density of small animals such as rodentia and insectivores will increase, especially that
of those small animals spreading natural focal infectious diseases like rats. This will increase
opportunities of these damned animals to contact human beings and their life necessities.
* Effects upon birds
There are many water ponds, lakes and rivers where wet land birds inhabit along roads under
planning. Since wet land birds seek for food and most of them nestle and reproduce on grassland,
shrub land or arbor, road construction will sure disturb and scare them and force them to migrate
from their habitats. But since road construction will be conducted in a relatively small area, it will
therefore make limited impact on those birds and the impact will end in a short time.
* Effects upon forest-dwelling animals
Road construction will, to some extent, cause damage to habitats of animals such as sparrow
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                  54



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPUI) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
birds, rats and small carnivores inhabiting grassland and shrub-land in part of plains and rolling
hills along the roads to be built.
During road construction, such activities as building builder's yard, builder's road and auxiliary
buildings, stacking raw materials and other activities of construction personnel may destroy and
reduce habitats of wildlives. Since roads to be built lie in plains and their vegetation types are
generally similar to each other, it is therefore not difficult for animals to find their new habitats. But
vegetation and ecological environment will be gradually restored when construction is completed.
(2)Hydrobiose
In light of a need for protecting water bodies flowing through roads to be built, no consideration will
be taken into piers to be built in water cross-section of these water bodies except the Zhujiahe
River when designing the project. Therefore, construction of the project will only have certain
impact on normal activities of fishes in the Zhujiahe River. Since fishes can bypass piers, bridges
to be built over the Zhujiahe River will block canals of fishes. With time passing by, the fishes will
adapt to their new environment.
By analogical analysis, it is not difficult to find that SS effects of construction of bridge base on
water body will be less than 60m for single pile. Except for increase of float quantity in part of water
areas, construction will exert no effect on large areas of water body. But since water quality in
areas which construction is involved in gets worse, quantity of bait organisms such as floating
organisms and benthonic animals will decrease and initial surviving, growth and reproducing
environment of fish will also change. Fish will be forced to migrate farther, thus reducing its
population density in these areas.
Since pile base construction can be completed in a short time, it is possible for construction to
avoid oviposition period of fish by adjusting operation time. At the same time, such measures as
protecting local areas and introducing advanced construction craft will be taken so as to reduce
effects of construction on aquatic organisms. Should water be kept plenty and clean as well as
taking other measures to protect fish when the project is completed, initial fish resources and their
habitats would not have a large change. This would not exert a big effect on type and quantity of
fish.
(3) Water and soil loss
For ground surface disturbed during road construction, water and soil loss will occur due to soil
loosening and rain flushing. Since areas along the line are plain, existing roads and land for
interchanges will be used as interim builder's yard and builder's road respectively. No more land is
needed to build interim construction facilities. Therefore, water and soil loss caused by the project
will derive mainly from excavating and filling of earth excavating yard, earth dumping yard and
road base.
(OFor the purpose of building of road base of the project, a large amount of earth will be obtained
from outside. The amount of earth from outside will total 360183m3 while that of earth needing to
be excavated out from construction field will reach 30347m3. According to the preliminary plan of
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                    55



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
earth fetching and dumping, earth for the project will be fetched from an earth dumping yard at one
side of North Chenjiaji Dike where comprehensive improvement project of the river mouth of the
Fuhe Riverlocates. While earth excavated from construction field will be dumped in that earth
dumping yard. When earth fetching and dumping construction is completed, landform, soil
structure of ground surface and vegetation of earth fetching and dumping yards will be destroyed.
That will destroy its initial water-holding capacity of ground surface, cause certain damage to local
ecological environment and rapidly fasten soil erosion. If it rains, rain water will flush ground
surface, thus resulting in water and soil loss of local construction sections. That is why water and
soil loss occur during project construction.
(9)During excavating, filling and forming construction of road base, vegetation of ground surface
and soil structure will be destroyed, thus leading to slopes. Owning to height difference between
road base and its two sides, surface runoff will be easy to form. Formed runoff will take away earth
particles and result in water and soil loss. Furthermore, such construction items necessary for
culvert construction of road bridges as pier hole drilling and base excavation will produce muck
piling. It is also unavoidable for earth and rock materials provisionally piled to cause part of water
and soil loss during periods of heavy rains and flood.

4.1.2 Analysis of Impact on Air Environment
(1) Dust
The dust during construction is mainly produced by the lime-soil mixing station and through the
transportation and handling of construction materials.
The lime-soil mixing station will be used in the project, where the lime-soil is mixed collectively
according to the design proportion. The mixed lime-soil will be conveyed to the construction site by
vehicles. Under the effect of wind force, the mixing operation will pollute the construction site with
TSP. According to the actual survey data of similar projects, the lime-soil 50m away from the down
wind of lime-soil mixing station is 8.90 mg/m3, 1.65 mg/m3 100m away and 0.3 mg/m3 150m away,
which conform to the secondary standard of Quality Standards of Air Environment
(GB3095-1996).
During construction, the transportation and handling of construction materials will pollute the areas
along the highway with TSP. According to the monitoring results of dust produced by vehicles on
similar construction sites, the dust 50m away from the down wind of lime-soil carrying vehicles is
11.625 mg/m3, 9.694 mg/m3 100m away and 5.093 mg/m3 150m away, which exceed the
secondary standard of Quality Standards of Air Environment (GB3095-1996). It can be seen that
the dust produced by the carrying vehicles will pollute the areas along the highway seriously.
It can be seen from the above analysis that the dust pollution produced in mixing of Lime-soil and
by the carrying vehicles cannot be ignored. Corresponding measures should be adopted to relieve
the pollution.
(2) Bitumen smoke during paving
In the project, the commercial bitumen concrete will be used to lay the pavement.
The bitumen smoke pollution in the project is mainly caused by hot-oil evaporation. During paving,
the gas is escaped from the hot materials pavement. Phenol about 60m away from the down wind
is s0.01 mg/m3 (The standard of former Soviet Union is 0.01 mg/m3); and THC about 60m away
is 0.16 mg/m3 (The standard of former Soviet Union is 0.16 mg/m3) . If equipped with smoke
prevention and dust control units, both the homemade and imported bitumen mixing stations are
able to satisfy the environmental protection requirements. To reduce the period during which the
sensitive places are affected, machine will be used for the paving of bitumen.
4.1.3 Analysis of Environmental Impact on Surface Water
(1) Domestic sewage
The domestic sewage during construction is mainly produced by the constructors.
The constructors are distributed along the highway and stay in a place only for a short period
of time, so the domestic sewage is scattered here and there, which will be treated in the septic
tank and used as fertilizer. So the domestic sewage will only have a little impact on the
environment.
The project is across Zhujiahe River, Huangxiaohe River, Jianshe Trench and Daijiashan
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection              57



The third ring north section (SAN  JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
Trench, etc. The domestic sewage of the constructors will be collected by the septic tanks and
used as fertilizer, which won't pollute the water body.
(2) Production sewage
The production sewage is mainly produced during the construction of bridges and
grade-separation pier column.
Only the piers of Zhujiahe River bridges need to be constructed in the water body. Other
bridges, flyover and grade-separation piers are not located in the water body.
Column piers and the foundation of bored pile should be adopted for the bridges and
grade-separation pier columns along the highway. The cast-in-place construction method should
be used for the construction of the deck and grade-separation pavement. The construction
technology of steel-plate-pile cylindrical cofferdam should be used for the construction of pier
bases under Zhujiahe River; and the construction technology of sandbag cloth anti-seepage
cofferdam sinking well should be used for the construction of piers on the banks of Zhujiahe River.
The construction of pier foundation of bridges will increase the SS at local water area. The
construction technology of cofferdam or sinking well is able to prevent water pollution effectively.
According to analogical analysis of dada, if the construction technology of cofferdam method is
adopted, the increment of SS 1 00m away from the construction site in the lower reaches will be no
more than 50mg/l, so the water quality in the water area more than 1 00m away won't be polluted.
After the completion of the project, the pollution within 100m in the lower reaches will also
disappear.
Generally speaking, during the construction of bored piles, if the construction site is shallow
water, the island built method is usually used for the construction of construction platform; if it is
deep water, the fixed plafform such as double-walled steel cofferdam platform will be adopted; and
if there is no or little ground water, the pored piles will be used. The method for treating slurry is:
Before boring, excavate the slurry pond. During boring, the soil and rock will be carried into the
slurry pond through the slurry cycling solid wall for sedimentation. After sedimentation, the slurry
will be reused. Regularly clean the sedimentation basin regularly and store the sediment
collectively. In this way, the slurry produced by the construction of bridges won't pollute the
farmland or water body.
