and a school, of which some residential quarters are no more than 5m away from the highway. It
can be concluded according to the predicted results that The impact of construction machinery
noises on some residential quarters at the daytime such as Daishan Villiage, Nanhu Villiage
(Group 20) , Nanhu Villiage (Group 21 ) and Nanhu Villiage (Xiaohekou) will exceed the
assessment standards and exceed the standards seriously at night. Therefore, the construction
unit should arrange the construction time rationally and avoid the construction of high-noise
machinery at the dense residential quarters at night to provide a favorable environment for the
residents.
4.1.5 The Solid Waste Produced by Construction
The solid waste during construction is mainly from the earthwork conveyed to other places,
demolished buildings and the domestic waste produced by the constructors.
The earthwork that needs to be conveyed to other places not more than 5 km away in the project
is about 30347m3. The comprehensive regulation works at the exit of Fuhe Riverwithin the
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                59



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN  to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
construction area of the project is under construction and its superfluous earth (about 827645m0,
most of which is stored inside Northern CHENJIAJI bank) can be used in the project. Therefore,
the earth conveyed to other places can be transported into the waste bank of the comprehensive
regulation works at the exit of FUHE River.
The demolished buildings in the project are about 2790m3, all of which can be used for the
protection of side slope of roadbed.
The domestic waste produced by the constructors is mainly stored near the storage yards,
construction camps, mixing stations and grade separation, etc.
The solid waste is distributed linearly along the highway, so if they are not stored or treated
properly, they will directly destroy the farm crops and vegetation and block up the irrigation ditches.
If they are stored too long and covered with dust, the dust will have impact on the nearby residents
in windy days. Furthermore, the waste can lead to the breeding of a large number of bacteria and
mosquito and thus increase the incidence of infectious diseases. The effluvium produced by the
waste will affect the living of residents as well as the landscapes. The highway to be constructed
will go across some rivers and trenches, so if not treated properly, the solid waste might worsen
the water quality. Therefore, during construction, the construction management should be
enhanced and the solid waste should be removed in time to reduce and even prevent such impact.
4.1.6 Analysis of Impact by Takeover of Land and Relocation of Residents
The construction of the project will inevitably occupy the land along the project. According to the
survey data during design period, 886.45 mu land needs to be permanently occupied in the project,
of which there is 350.77 mu cultivated land accounting for 39.6%; 222.51 mu land used for
building, accounting for 25.1 %; 313.28 mu water surface, accounting for 35.3%.
The farmland occupied will lose its output functions forever and directly affect the living of the
farmers. Although the total farmland occupied is not much and won't affect the agricultural
economy seriously, as far as the farmers involved are concerned, their means of production may
be lack and their living will be affected, so it is necessary to carry out rational compensation and
relocation.
54877m2 of houses needs to be demolished in the project, involving 1,297 people. The living area,
quality of life, living habit and their social relations of these people will be affected, so it is
necessary to carry out rational compensation and relocation.

4.2.2 Analysis of Impact on Ecological Environment
(1) Terrestrial organism
(O) Impact on terrestrial animals
During operation, the man-made impediments and environmental pollution caused by the project
will impact the terrestrial animals.
Because the land is occupied, the animals have to seek new living environments and thus the
inter-specific competition is enhanced. Besides, the man-made impediments caused by the
highway will limit the home range of animals, so the plants whose seeds are spread by the animals
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                   70



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
and insects will also be affected.
The highway mainly occupied the farmland, so it only has little impact on the animals. The
amphibians along the highway mainly inhabit the farmlands, streams and brushwood and most of
their species are closely related to human activities. Some birds will migrate to adjacent areas.
Part of the habitat of some birds and the rats of Galliformes inhabiting the brushwood and grass,
the small animals of Carnivora and the reptiles will be destroyed; however, they have the abilities
to migrate and their food sources are diversified, so the project won't impact their inhabiting
greatly.
During operation, the highway will be closed all the way and there will be more and more vehicles.
The amphibians and reptiles like to immigrate between the wetland and highland. They move very
slowly, so when they pass through the expressway at night, they might be collided and even killed
by the vehicles passing by. However, the culverts at the roadbed can be used for the animals to
immigrate, which reduces the probability of being collided and killed in the expressway.
Furthermore, the noise pollution and tail gas exhausted will reduce the quality of living
environment of the animals, so they have to seek other habitats far away from the highway.
(9) Impact on terrestrial plant
After the project is build, the vegetation in the farmland permanently occupied will be completely
destroyed and replaced by the pavement and its auxiliary facilities. Among the vast piece of
farmland, the pavement and its auxiliary facilities form a belt-form space, which will change the ray
radiation, temperature, humidity and wind, etc. Such change of microclimate will accordingly lead
to the change of plants, the animals and microorganisms at the edge of farmland. According to
study, the edge's impact on the microclimate can extend from the edge to 15-60m away. Due to
edge effect, within 60m away from the highway on both sides, the species in the community will
change: the existing tolerant evergreen shrub and herb will be gradually replaced by sun plant or
semi-sun plant and the space near the highway will be occupied by strong sun shrub and weed.
(2) Aquatic organism
During operation, the runoff rainwater in the deck might lead to the rise in concentration of
petroleum and COD in the water body of rivers. According to analogical estimate, during normal
operation, there will only be a little COD to be released, which can be absorbed by the
self-purification ability of the water body. Furthermore, the probability of accidents during the
carriage of dangerous goods in the deck is very small. However, once any accident occurs, there
will be serious impact, so the control and monitoring over the vehicles for the carriage of
dangerous goods will be enhanced and effective emergency scheme will be formulated to avoid
damage to aquatic organisms.
Besides, the traffic noises, lighting at night and human activities during operation will affect the
normal inhabiting environment of fish and some zoobenthos to certain degree and even drive
them away. However, the water area involved in the highway is very small relative to the rivers, so
the project will have just a little impact on the aquatic organisms and won't make the fish and
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection             71



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Rond drainage project environment influence statement (for opprovot)
zoobenthos die out.
(3) Water and soil losses
After the project is built, the driveways will be water-proof bitumen pavement; and from the
marginal strip to the red line are greening belt or slope protection works and side ditch. The
exposed area is small, so the water and soil losses can be effectively controlled.
4.2.3 Prediction and Analysis of Impact on Air Environment
During operation, the main pollutants of air environment are NOx in the tail gas of vehicles. The
analogical analysis method will be used to analyze the impact of NO2 on surrounding air
environment. Take the sub-section within the territory of EZHOU (ZELIN) of WUHAN-HUANGSHI
section of YICHANG-HUANGSHI expressway as the analysis object.
Considering that the NO2 factor has always been used in the prediction of impact on air pollution in
the previous highway projects and that the pollution of NOx is similar with that of NO2, so we will
use NOx and corresponding standard value to carry out anagogic analysis in the project.
The data used for analogical analysis is obtained by Hubei Provincial Academy of Environmental
Sciences through the actual monitoring for five consecutive days respectively before and after the
construction of the sub-section within the territory of EZHOU (ZELIN) of WUHAN-HUANGSHI
section of YICHANG-HUANGSHI expressway. The monitoring factor is NOX and the monitoring
results can be seen in Table 4-9.
The monitoring results show that 40m away from the highway, the average concentration of NOx
per hour is 0.67%-24.67% of the "hourly average value" of the standard value. So it can be
concluded that the concentration of NOx on both sides of highway satisfied the secondary
standard of Quality Standards of Air Environment (GB3095-1996). Thus, it is concluded in this
assessment that during operation, the NO2 contained in the tail gas exhausted by the vehicles on
the highway won't exceed the standards.

4.2.4 Analysis of Environmental Impact on Surface Water
The highway construction project belongs to development non-pollution ecological construction
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                72



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
project. It also needs to cross through some rivers and farmiand, but the bridges and culverts wil
be built, so the direct pollution on the water body can be avoided.
If no accidents occur, the runoff sewage in the deck is able to flow into the river and trench along
the side ditch and the pavement runoff is able to flow into the trenches along the drainage ditches
on both sides of the highway.
During operation, the main sewage is the surface runoff produced by rainwater. The pollutants in
the tail gas of vehicles, the particles produced by wearing of vehicle tyres, the clay in the vehicle
frame, the pollutants falling to the pavement during vehicle brake and the oil leaked from the
vehicles due to weak operating condition will flow into the drainage system of the highway and
finally into the surface water body along the pavement runoff produced by rainfall. The main
pollutants include petroleum, organic and suspended matter, which may pollute the water body.
There are many factors affecting the pavement runoff pollution, including rainfall, duration of
rainfall, the pavement and air pollution concerning vehicle flow rate, the internal time between two
rainfalls, width of pavement, sedimentation of dust, drought period and length of section of
highway accepting pollution. Besides, these factors are variable, random and occasional, so there
is no universally applicable method at present that can be used to compute the runoff pollution.
(1) Analysis of concentration of runoff pollutants of pavement
South China Institute of Environmental Sciences of State Environmental Protection Administration
of China once carried out experimentation for the pavement runoff pollution in Southern China with
the following testing method: Adopt artificial rainfall to form pavement runoff; the interval time
between the rainfall for two times is 20d; the vehicle flow rate and rainfall are already known; the
duration of rainfall is 1h; the rainfall intensity is 81.6mm; and the samples are collected for several
times within 1h. The measurement value of the pavement pollutants can be seen in Table 4-10.
Table 4-10 Measurement Value of Concentration of Runoff Pollutants of Pavement
Items          5-20min         20-40min        40-60min       Average value
SS (mg/l)     231.42~-158.52   158.52-90.36    90.36--18.71        100
BOD (mg/i)      7.34-7.30        7.30-4.15       4.15-1.26          5.08
Oil (mg/I)     22.30-19.74      19.74-3.12      3.12-0.21         11.25
It can be seen from Table 4-10 that from the beginning of rainfall and the formation of runoff (about
30min), the concentration of suspended matter and oil in the rainwater is high and then begins to
decline rapidly; 40-60min after the beginning of rainfall, the pavement has been rinsed out
basically and the concentration of pavement runoff pollutants is stabilized in a low level.
(2) Analysis of runoff of pavement
The runoff of pavement can be computed according to the following formula:

According to computation, the pavement runoff caused by the project is about 287,000.00m3/a, all
of which will flow into the new river way of Fuhe Riverthrough the pumping stations along the
highway. It is concluded in the assessment that relative to the conveyance capacity of FUHE River,
the pavement runoff during the operation of the project will only have a little impact on the water
body of FUHE River.
If any accidents occur due to weak operating conditions of vehicles, the gasoline and engine oil
may leak to pollute the pavement. Then when it rains, the rainwater containing petroleum and
COD will flow into and pollute the nearby water area through the drain trunk. Therefore, the traffic
control should be enhanced to avoid accidents.
(3) Analysis of drainage of grade-separation pumping station
O Displacement
According to the annual average rainfall in WUHAN, suppose that all the rainwater forms surface
runoff (the rainwater absorbed by the pavement is not considered), then within the catchments of
the grade-separation pumping stations of the project, the displacement of rainwater of each
grade-separation pumping station is about 7600m3/a, totaling 45600m3/a for six pumping stations.
(©) Water quality
Among the passages where the six pumping stations are located, there are four vehicle
passages and one railway passage (across Beijing-Guangzhou Railway in THIRD RING ROAD) .
Except the railway passage, all passages adopt reinforced concrete frame construction placed in
situ. Therefore, the quality of the rainwater collected by the pumping stations is similar to that of
the rainwater in highway as Table 4-10.
(a) Destination
The rainwater will be pumped to nearby open drainage ditches or rainwater system and finally flow
into FUHE River.
4.3 Analysis of Accidental Risks
If no strict management is executed or the transportation personnel fail to operate correctly, the
traffic accidents may occur. The vehicle loading hazardous chemicals suffers traffic accidents; the
hazardous chemicals may leak and pollute the environment. The pollution caused by traffic
accidents mainly refers to the pollution of water body below the highway.
After the project is built, the transportation condition in the area will be greatly improved and the
traffic volume will be increased. Along with the development and utilization of the land along the
hiQhwav, the vehicle flow rate will increase obviously and the aoods to be conveyed will be also
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               74



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN  to PING  ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
diversified, which increases the possibility of accidents to certain degree.
4.3.1 Analysis of Accidental Risk Sources
A number of research findings show that the water pollution accidents are mainly caused by traffic
accidents. When the accident site is over or across the water area, the pollutants may pollute the
water body. The types of water pollution accidents can be divided into:
(1) The gasoline (or diesel oil) and engine oil of the vehicles leak and flow into the nearby water
body;
(2)The vehicles loading hazardous chemicals suffer traffic accidents and the hazardous chemicals
leak and flow into the nearby water body;
(3) Suffering traffic accidents in the deck, the vehicles and goods fall into the rivers.
4.3.2 Prediction of Accidental Risks
According to analogical computation, the probability of accidents in the highway in the near and far
future is only 0.010-0.033 time/a, which shows that during operation, the probability of serious
traffic accidents suffered by the vehicles loading hazardous chemicals is very low.
4.4 Analysis of Compliance with Urban Planning
It is put forward in the Overall Plan of WUHAN City (1996-2020) that: "According to the natural
conditions and layout of main urban area, the planned road system should follow the following
principles: The roads in HANKOU, HANYANG and WUCHANG should form their own systems;
and the radiated roads combined with rings and square grids should be adopted, which are made
up of quick-speed roads, trunk roads, secondary trunk roads and local roads. The quick-speed
roads at the main urban area consist of 3 ring roads and 10 radiated roads connecting with the
national and provincial highways".
It is advanced in the Outline of the Eleventh Five-Year Overall Plan of National Economy and
Social Development of WUHAN City: "The construction of comprehensive traffic network in
WUHAN should be quickened and the road traffic system should be improved; the inner ring roads
should be normal, the secondary ring roads should be built, the third ring roads should be linked
up and the outer ring roads should be perfected; the openness of the road system in central urban
area should be enhanced and the accesses to WUHAN City in eastern and western HANKOU,
Southern HANYANG and Southeastern WUCHANG should be built; the main road system and
local road system at development zone should be perfected according to the layout of
'combination of ring and network and axial radiation to form the main road network of 'four rings
and thirteen radiated roads and expand the urban space; The network road construction should be
enhanced and the compound traffic consisting of quick-speed roads, trunk roads and track traffic
should be built between the central urban area and development zones".
The THIRD RING ROAD goes along ZHANGGONG Bank at HANKOU, then spans HANJIANG

5. Pollution Control Measures and Proposals
With further improvement of environmental laws and regulations, in particular the implementation
of "three-simultaneousness" system for construction projects, highway construction projects has
accumulated mature environmental control measures in design, construction and operation period,
which all are technically feasible; in consideration of large investment in highway projects and
environmental protection measures' accounting for a low proportion of investments, environmental
protection will follow the principle of phased implementation so as to realize economic investment,
reasonable technology, operational and environmental benefits.
From analysis of the project's impact upon the environment, environmental pollution linkages
arising from the construction mainly include temporary water, air and sound effects, and pollution
prevention focuses on further management and supervision, including organization and
management of working procedures and environmental protection publicity and education for
construction staff. All management and supervision requirements in relation to environmental
works and environmental protection shall be followed by the contractors.
5.1 Pollution Prevention Measures and Proposals during Construction Period
5.1.1 Civilization Construction Management
As indicated in the above analysis, in case of improper management or prevention measures
during construction period, it is extremely easy to produce a wide range of serious pollution and
thus to affect the people's health, the quality of living environment and surrounding environment.
Therefore, construction unit shall carry out civilized construction fully in accordance with "Civilized
Construction Regulations for Wuhan City's Construction Projects", which, on one hand, can
beautify Wuhan City, and on the other hand, can reduce the pollution during construciton period
and reduce the pollution upon the environment and the impact upon living environment of
sensitive populations. Civilization construction management covers the construction site fencing,
materials storage and transport, temporary facilities, safety facilities, construction noise control,
waste treatment, sewage drainage, management of surrounding environment, etc.
(1) Construction unit's Project Manager (Project Chief) shall take overall responsibility for the
management in the construction process, and shall establish and organize the implementation of
civilization construction responsibility system on basis of the project scale, technical dificulty and
specific conditions in the construction site.
Construction unit (or Supervision Company) shall be responsible for the works which shall be
undertaken by construction unit as specified in the contract.
(2) The project's construction shall be carried out within approved scope of construction site;
expansion of construction site or road occupation is required with examination and approval
procedures at competent authorities according to relevant laws, regulations and norms.
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               77



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
Approved construction site and temporary road occupation shall not be excavated or used for
other purposes by construction unit without permission.
Construction unit shall set up temporary storage facilities for construction equipments and
materials according to general layout plan; no building materials or machinery can be stored
outside the fence of cosntruction site without approval.
(3) Construction unit must prepare construction signs at visible points in the site, which shall
indicate the project name, hierarchical structure, area, commencement/completion date,
construction unit, designer, supervisor, and name of the person in charge of the project.
(4) Construction site must have fence; the fence for the sites nearby residential area and major
roads shall be at least 2m high. The fence shall be solid, clean and beautiful.
(5) For pile foundation works using boring placement techniques, construction site shall be taken
with such measrues as soil drop or hard terrace coverage to prevent spillover of the slurry.
(6) Construction site entrance/exit shall be prepared with transport vehicle washing and drainage
facilities in compliance with the standards and norms.
(7) Construction unit shall properly treat construction wastewater and take effective measures to
ensure the access to roads at construction site entrance/exit. Drainage system shall be in good
condition and the site shall be clean.
Flush slurry in the construction shall not be directly discharged into the city's drainage system
without treatment. No harmful waste shall be used for backfill.
(8) Safety passage shall be prepared where vehicles or pedestrian passes through in the site.
Protection devices shall be provided for ditches, wells, grooves, bores, pile holes, etc.
(9) Construction site shall be provided with employees' living facilities corresponding to the
project's scale. Employees' living facilities must conform to sanitation, ventilation, lighting and
other requirements.
(10) Mixing station shall be adopted with canopy-type dustproof measures, and blocking shall be
provided on the windward side.
al) Building and living garbage arising from the construction shall be timely cleaned. Such flying
building materials and waste as transport fluid and sand stone shall be sealed and covered without
scattering along the line. Transport vehicles shall be cleaned before leaving the site so as to
prevent the mud on vehicles from polluting the roads.
For disposal of construction sediment, construction unit shall go through examination and
approval procedures in advance at the city's sanitation authority in accordance with relevant
provisions, and shall dispose them in compliance with quantity, transport route, time and dumping
site.
(an In addition to emergency repair and rescue, it is not allowed to use pile hammers, breakers,
bulldozers, excavators, rammers, generators, electric saws, electric concrete vibrators or engage
in other works with environmental noise pollution in case of the construction in residential areas,
education areas, sanitarial areas and other areas in need of quiet environment at night (from 22:00
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                   78



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
to 6:00 the next day). No operation of high-noise equipments at night if the project construciton is
carried out nearby sensitive points along the line.
For the construction at night which can not avoid noise pollution due to the production process
continuity or other special reasons, construction unit must in advance hold the certification issued
by competent authority and report to the environmental protection authority and the City's
government for examination and approval.
(12 During the suspension, construction unit shall keep the fence and entrance/exit in clear
conditions and the shops nearby the street neat and beautiful.
03) Daily cleaning shall be carried out in construction site, and the site shall be cleaned
immediately after the completion without scattering of buidling waste. After the completion of the
project, construction unit shall remove the site fence and temporary facilities as well as materilas
and garbages left in the site within one month.
5.1.2 Protection and Restoration Measures for Ecological Environmental during
Construction Period
(1) Protection measures and proposals for terrestrial plants
(0 Measures to avoid ecological impact
The method to avoid ecological impact is to take appropriate measures to maximum adverse
ecological impacts. Measures to avoid ecological impact are aimed at absolute protection of the
environment with important ecological functions. Generally such measures as change of the
project site, engineering, construction plan, road rebuilding, change of the project's content or
scale are taken to prevent the project from causing irreparable damage to the environment.
For spill pit and temporary stock yard, strip off 30cm topsoil on the surface, stack collectively, take
interim protection measures to prevent loss of nutrients, prepare bagged soil around topsoil for
temporary blocking, and spread red clover seeds onto blocking surface for temporary protection.
Set up the drains around, set up sedimentation pond at lower parts around the drains, and
discharge into downstream river channel or nearby ditches after settling sediment in water flow. At
the end of spoil, remove temporary block, evenly spread stripping topsoil onto sediment face and
top, carry out rolling down and second plowing of sediment top, and keep protective measures for
slope plants in consistence with external platform.
For temporary land use like construction camps, first strip off surface mellow soil], store in the
court, tamp down stack slope, use bagged soil as provisional block, spread red clover seeds on
the surface to prevent loss of nutrients, and use as surface soil after the completion of construction;
excavate drains around each camp, connect drains to nearby river channel or natural drains, and
make sure to arrange fulltime person to be responsible for the de-silting of drains in rainy season;
at the end of construction, for new requisite temporary farmland, remove hardened layer resulting
from construction camp, carry out leveling and second plowing, spread red clover seeds onto
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                 79



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
stripping topsoil for temporary protection, return topsoil at the end of construction, plant poplars
and spread seeds.
() Measures to reduce ecological impact
The reduction of ecological impact is to take proper measures for inevitable adverse ecological
impacts to alleviate the affected scope and extent. Generally the reduction of ecological impact is
to minimize the loss through advanced ecological design method.
Upon construction nearby farmland, construction activities shall be conducted within the scope of
land requisition, and the scope of construction roads and temporary occupation zone shall be
minimized. Reduce farmland occupation and strengthen tree and grass protection.
Temporary stock yard, construction vehicles, newly-built temporary roads and newly-built
construction camps shall be arranged in a concentrative way, and every effort shall be made to
ensure no scattered arrangement; living garbage of construction staff shall be transported outside
the site after uniform treatment, and make sure no chucking or damage of crops.
(a) Measures to restore and compensate ecological impact
Vegetation protection measures mainly deals with restoration of vegetation, for which the project's
vegetation restoration and reconstruction technologies and measures are very important.
According to the local climate, attention shall be paid to the following main technical points in
relation to the vegetation restoration measures:
According to the national forest laws and other related regulations, in the planning of road
landscape, the area of reconstructed vegetation shall not be less than the original area, through
which the ecosystem around the roads can be in stable condition. In addition to selection of locally
suitable trees, attention shall be paid to the staggering distribution of different species in the
course of vegetation restoration and compensation so as to improve the diversity of plant species
along the road, to enhance disease resistance and the corridor stability. Moreover, tree selection
shall go through strict quarantine to prevent the introduction of disease.
() Measures and proposals for highway landscape
Restoration of the vegetation within the scope of highway land: strengthen construction
management, make no damage of the vegetation outside or minimize the damage, and for the
restoration of vegetation along the roads, in addition to roadbed protection, it is necessary to
consider highway landscape and environment protection (such as noise reducing, air pollution
prevention, etc.) and to satisfy traffic safety (no barrier towards sight of drivers so as to ensure
normal driving) so as to realize the combination of landscape, beautification and environmental
protection.
Embankment, cutting and slope: sod for embankment, cutting and slope shall be selected to be
perennial grass lawns with local drought resistance, abundant root systems, easy survival, fast
growth and good soil reinforcement.
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                80



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
Slag yard and temporary occupation zone: after reconstruction of slag yard and deep plowing ot
temporary occupation zone, those not used as farmland shall be planted to restore the vegetation,
and green shelterbelt shall be built around farmland on basis of local farmland network.
Selection of grass and trees: in principle of "planting trees and grass according to local conditions",
trees and grass shall be selected after a detailed investigation of terrain, soil and climatic
conditions, focusing upon local fine trees with the introduction of new species, so as to guarantee
the survival rate.
( Control measures for ecological impact
During the construction period, mainly monitor the construction area involved in sensitive points; it
is also necessary to strengthen the investigation of regional distribution of plant protection, to
notify competent departments immediately after finding important protection objects in the
construction and to relocate for protection. During the operation period, mainly monitor habitat
changes, vegetation changes and overall changes in the ecosystem. Strengthen ecological
management through monitoring, set up ecological environment management staff, establish
management and reporting system, carry out environmental impact education, improve the
environmental awareness of construction staff and management staff, and go towards beneficial
or healthy ecological environment through dynamic monitoring and management improvement.
(2) Protection measures for terrestrial animals
(O) Measures to avoid ecological impact
Improve protection consciousness of construction staff, and forbid the hunting of wild animals.
Construction personnel must abide by "Wild Animal Protection Law of The People's Republic of
China", no hunting of wild animals in the construction area and the surrounding, particularly no
hunting of national protected animals in the construction, neither construction workers nor local
residents are allowed to kill wildlife.
Investigate construction periods and methods, and prevent noise impact upon wildlife. Most wild
birds and mammals go out for feeding in the morning, evening or night, and the birds rest in the
noon. In order to reduce construction noise's disturbance upon wildlife, a good planning of
construction method and time shall be carried out, and every effort shall be made to avoid the
noise impact in the morning and noon.
(® Measures to reduce ecological impact
During the construction period, strengthen borrow pit, spoil pit and slag yard, and enhance the
management of construction personnel. Construction staff living sewage shall not be directly
drained into the surrounding water so as to reduce water pollution and the impact upon animal
habitats.
( Measures to restore and compensate ecological impact

The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment inftnence statement (for approval)
Do a good job of the restoration of ecological environment after the completion of the project as
soon as possible so as to minimize adverse impact upon the animals resulting from the destruction
of habitat.
Crowed green belts are prepared at bridge location to prevent adverse effect upon animals
resulting from lights and noise, and the restoration of underneath vegetation and natural
landscape shall be enhanced to help animals adapt to new habitat.
(A Control measures for ecological impact
Strengthen management and reduce pollution; as there is a large proportion of agricultural
vegetation in the evaluation area with many muse or plagues, attention shall be paid to preventing
people, livestock and construction staff outside the evaluation area from snakebite or plague injury.
A new landscape of muntains, water, forests and birds will come together with the construction of
roads and forestation.
(3) Protection measures for aquatic organisms
Aquatic organisms involved in the project' waters are the species widely distributed in nearby
similar environment, and change in environment after the completion of the project will certainly
result in change or disappear of aquatic biological populations in some local waters. However,
species resources will not be severely damaged, and no effect will be posed upon preservation of
the species.
Prior to the project's construction, do a good job of pre-construction planning; during the
construction, strengthen the protection of slag yard and water environment, avoid the pollution of
local waters along the line, and minimize the impact upon aquatic biological environmental. Do a
good job of the restoration of the ecological environment after the completion, and reduce adverse
impact upon water quality and aquatic organisms.
5.1.3 Control Measures for Air Pollution during Construction Period
(1) Construction materials passing through urban and rural settlements and other environmentally
sensitive sections shall be done with regular cleaning and watering according to transport and
weather conditions so as to reduce secondary road dust, and each section shall be at least
equipped with a sprinkler (purchased or leased); generally water spreading once in morning
(7:30-8:30), noon (12:00-13:00) and night (17:00-18:00) respectively, and water spreading every
two hours shall be conducted when the wind speed is above Grade 3 or fine weather in summer.
(2) Construction material transport vehicle shall be adopted with the combination of decked
sheeting and wet combined so as to reduce dust pollution, and stacked materials shall be covered,
and transport vehicle running routes shall keep away from settlements and environmental
sensitive sections as possible.
(3) Storage yard and mortar mixing station for highway Construction shall stay away from
residential areas or other densely populated area, and shall be placed in a open area. Storage
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               82



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
yard and mortar mixing station shall be 300m outside downward wind direction of main residential
areas along the line so as to reduce dust pollution towards the residents.
5.1.4 Control measures for sewage pollution during construction period
(1) Management measures
Carry out water environment protection education on construction sites and camps, make workers
understand the importance of water environment protection; particularly in the construction of
river-crossing bridge substructure, construction shall be made in the dry season as possible;
meanwhile, strengthen construction management and supervision regularly inspect construction
machinery, and prevent water body pollution from oil leakage. Construction materials such as
asphalt, oil and chemicals shall be stacked nearby surface water body and shall be provided with
temporary shelter; necessary measures shall be taken to prevent soil and bulk construction
material from blocking drains or existing irrigation ditches and water mains.
(2) Disposal of construction slurry and other solid waste
Minimize the sewage arising from the roadbed and bridge construction directly flowing into rivers
and irrigation channels so as to reduce the concentration of water suspended solids; dispose pile
foundation construction slurry, transport the slurry arising from caisson dredger sank, water
surface and land-based drilling pile construction to the place designated by construction unit for
disposal, selection of slurry disposal station is required with the consent of local authorities.
Sludge from bridge pier foundation excavation shall be shipped to the designated storage location
without random disposal, and it is recommended to use nearby borrow pit for spoil. Household
garbage shall be centrally collected and cleaned by the municipal sanitation department.
(3) Sewage treatment measures during construction period
Construction camp's impact on water environment mainly comes from sewage discharge, and the
impact upon water body is related to the number of construction workers. Since there is no
municipal network along the line and supporting regional sewage treatment plant has not been put
into operation, no construction wastewater shall be directly discharged into natural water body;
construction site for water-crossing sections shall stay away from water body edge, and all
sewage shall go through septic tank before the discharge. In consideration that agricultural land is
mainly used during the construction along the line, all sewage in septic tank is recommended to
use as agricultural fertilizer.
(4) Disposal of concrete mixing wastewater and oil sewage
Concrete mixing process will result in a limited number of SS-alkaline wastewater, and
sedimentation tank (sizing 3 x 5 x 2m) shall be arranged at concrete mixing yard for wastewater
collection and treatment. Construction of bored piles will also produce slurry water, and
sedimentation ponds and ditches shall be built for recycle.
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                 83



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment inflnence statement (for approval)
5.1.5 Control Measures for Noise Pollution during Construction Period
(1) Maximize the use of low noise machinery, construction machinery equipments shall be
conducted with noise measurement in advance under regular work conditions, and no access to
the site shall be allowed for the machinery going beyond national standards. During the
construction, the equipments shall also be done with regular maintenance, so as to avoid the
noise increase due to poor equipments.
(2) Compared with the operation period, the construction period is of short-term noise impacts,
which mainly deals with the interference towards residents in night construction, therefore, no
high-noise machinery night (22:00 -6:00 next day) construction shall be allowed; Road
construction nearby schools shall be adjusted properly; construction time shall be arranged on
holidays or after schooling, or temporary noise reduction measures are taken, such as wooden
panels and so on.
(3) In accordance with "Noise Limits for Construction Boundary", construction boundary shall be
rationally determined. As many villages along the line are close to highway, every effort shall be
made to avoid that construction camps is set up nearby the villages.
(4) If existing roads in the construction site are used to transport construction materials, and
attention shall be paid to reasonable arrangement of transport time for construction materials,
which, on the one hand, minimizes the impact upon residents' night rest and students' schooling,
on the other hand, poses no impact upon original roads. In addition, transport vehicles shall slowly
pass through villages and school without whistle, and construction roads to be newly built shall be
stay away from the towns and other sensitive buildings.
5.1.6 Measures to Resolve the Effect from Land Requisition and Demolition
The construction unit is deeply concerned of the impact which may be placed upon the people
along the line by land requisition and demolition of the project, and has prepared a resettlement
plan according to the requirements of World Bank OP4.12 policies and the policies of the state
and Hubei Province in relation to demolition and resettlement. The plan will provide reasonable
compensation for the demolition from the project's land use, reasonably arrange the affected
people, and set up specialized agencies to formulate detailed plans, to fulfill land requisition and
demolition work, to minimize the impact from the project upon the residents along the line, and to
improve the residents' living level correspondingly instead of being dropped in the project
construction so that the residents can benefit from the project.
Below is the introduction of some measures to resolve the adverse impacts arising from the
project's land requisition and demolition, which is mainly quoted from the demolition and
resettlement plan report.
(1) Compensation
According to relevant laws, regulations and standards of the state and Hubei Province and World
Bank OP4.12 policies, land requisition and demolition for the proposed project will be reasonably

(2) Resettlement
Based on resettlement wills of the affected people through socio-economic survey and the
characteristics of the project's location at the city edge and mostly being rural collective villagers
among the affected people, the project will resettle the people in combination of money and object
placement.
(0 Resettlement of the affected urban residents
Those in favor of monetary compensation for resettlement will be timely paid with housing
relocation compensation, indoor facilities compensation, re-housing expenses, transition costs
compensation, etc. after the signing of resettlement compensation agreement, and those who
relocate within the specified period will paid with advance relocation incentives. All compensation
will be directly paid to the affected people after handling payment procedures at designated banks.
Those in favor of object placement will be provided with sufficient economic housing and
second-hand housing stock information for selection of the affected people. As the site locates at
Houhu, a new residential area for Wuhan City planning, which has 30-40 newly-built and
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection              86



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
to-be-built residential quarters with a total of 300,000 residents and complete auxiliary facilities.
The area is a new resident quarter which is the most nearest to the downtown, and the current
housing price is RMB3,000 per square meters. It is a residential area with high cost performance,
and has large amunt of housing stock and house types, and thus is very suitable for selection of
the affected people at various levels according to their own needs. Those in favor of economic
housing will not be restricted by Wuhan Economic Housing Purchase Qualifications, and thus can
buy quite satisfactory houses. Moreover, the north of the project, namely north of central
circumferential line, currently belongs to the outskirts of Wuhan City -- Huangpi District. Despite a
stone's throw, there is a sharp difference of current real estate prices, and house price in Huangpi
District is about RMB2,000 per square meters, which is a good choice for resettlement of those
low/ middle-income families.
(® Resettlement of the affected rural villagers
Those in favor of monetary compensation (usually the houses are not entirely demolished or other
houses in the village exist) will be timely compensated as urban residents.
Those in favor of object resettlement, Resettlement Office and the district's governmental
departments and street offices will discuss together and convene villagers' congress to select
reasonable re-housing place nearby. A housing area of 80-1 00 square meters is available for the
affected villagers for each household.
Costs of "road connection, power supply and water supply and ground leveling" of all housing area
will be borne by the project office.
®) Resettlement for the affected enterprises
A total of five houses in relation to the affected units of the project will obtain monetary
compensation (including housing compensation and compensation for business loss), moreover,
they are allowed to build business shops for proper resettlement. After the completion of the
project, the traffic situation in the area will be improved greatly, from which marketing companies
and other enterprises will greatly benefit, and the operating situation is greatly improved. See
Table 5 -4 for resettlement of the affected enterprises.

(3) Implementation department and progress
The project is implemented by Road & Infrastructure Construction Office, and resettlement work is
covered by Resettlement Department. Socio-economic survey will be conducted from in early
March to early April 2007, mobilization and coordination and public participation will be conducted
from April to May, land requisition and demolition will e started in June, land requisition will be
completed in March 2008, and demolition will be completed in June 2008. The entire project will
be completed by the end of 2008.
(4) Internal and external monitoring
Wuhan University Research Center of Engineering Resettlement, the external monitoring unit of
the project, has already involved in early monitoring. Internal monitoring staff also has started an
internal monitoring. Monitoring contents and indexes are the same as Wuhan Urban Traffic Project,
and the monitoring report will be submitted together with resettlement monitoring report for the
Wuhan Urban Traffic Project.
Complaint and appeal procedures and methods for resettlement work of the project are the same
as those in resettlement plan of Wuhan Urban Traffic Project.
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               88



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
5.2 Pollution Controls & Preventions in Operation
5.2.1  Air Pollution Control & Preventions
Vehicles' tail gas pollution control relies on on governmental supervision and manangment of the
road administrations as the project is an public urban transportation facility avaialbe for all the
vehicels that meet relevant requirements.
(1) Implement existing control measures for tail gas emission
Series of measures have been taken to control emission in Wuhan
(X) Sample check new vehicles on the roads and implement emission acceptance check;
(® Distribution and use of ethanol gasoline within urban; lead gasoline shall be forbidden;
® Reclaim wasted motor vehicles in accordance with Chinese Automobile Gas Emission
Standard allowing no reselling or transfer;
() Implement annual check and sample check system and control excessive emission;
($) Keep vehicle increase under control, including taxi, autobike and electric vehicles; stop issuing
additional autobikes license plates in Wuhan.
These measures will help alleviate air pollution and control the vehicles driven on the road
constructed.
(2) Implement vehicles gas emission control strategy
Integrate the gas emission control strategy with the municipal gas pollution strategy, establish M/l
system, tail gas emission research & monitoring center, automatic monitoring system and set one
or two gas emission monitoring points on both sides of the road which will be connected with
Wuhan automatic monitoring points network so as to realize the road real-time monitoring.
(3)Adopt proper measures to control tail gas emission
Build greening belt to control gas emission after completion of the project
O  Plant rosebay, camphor tree and other trees in vacant land that could absorb noxious
substance from tail gas.
(© Improve vehicles management, stop vehicles in poor conditions or overloaded driving on the
road, conduct regular maintenance on the road to ensure it is in good conditions to reduce the
pollutant emissions from vehicles running on poorly maintained road.
5.2.2  Noise Control & Preventions
During operation series of measures shall be taken including noise reduction, project
management and route planning control to guarantee better acoustic environment on both sides of
the road.
(1 )Noise Reduction
In China noise reductions include noise proof barrier, resettlement, sound proof window and noise
reduction trees. See T5-6 for their advantages and disadvantages.

(2) Project management
lImprove the road transportation including restricting vehicles in poor conditions to run on the
Ring and setting the sign of speed limitation or No Horn in the both sides of the roads to effectively
control traffic noise pollution
(®) Maintain the road regularly to guarantee smoothness so as to prevent the extra noise due to
poor road condition.
(3) Requirement of planning design control
(DResidential areas along the line shall be rebuilt far from the Ring and kept from the line in a safe
distance (normally 200m from the centerline) by referring to the roadside Noise Prediction Scope
and based on the local geological conditions. Newly built housings shall be kept from the line in a
safe distance too otherwise the builders shall be responsible for the noise control.
(®) The noise sensitive receivers including schools, hospitals, health center shall be built beyond
250m of the road so as to achieve better sound quality.
5.3 Traffic accident control
Efforts shall be taken to make sure that goods especially chemicals are well packaged and safely
transported, the road is under organized control and other precautions are taken to minimize and
eliminate accidents.
5.3.1  Packaging and Transportation of Dangerous Materials
Hazardous materials transportation shall be strictly conducted in accordance with the relevant
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                 93



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
requirements of Regulations of Dangerous Cargo Transportation (TI 3130).
The containers of dangerous materials shall be secured, sealed and identified with labels and
designations in accordance with GB 190 Labels for Packages of Dangerous Goods. Noxoius
data(flash point and melting point), fireproofing, explosion protection, fire extinguisher, safty
transportation and explosives physcial change of combustibles shall be noted on the speicification
before being shipped.
Vehicles transporting hazardous articles shall present certificates and obtain approval from
relevant communication authorities. Articles transported shall be those specified on the bill.
Vehicles transporting hazardous articles not specified on the List of Dangerous Goods shall
present technical approval issued by competent authorities.
The persons in charge of load and unload shall wear protective clothes and work with care; they
may not throw, draw, press or scrape goods or damage containers, keep label intact and place
them in safety.
5.3.2 Road Management and Maintenance
(1)The line will cross Huangxiaohe River, Jianche Canal, Daijiahan Canal, Zhujiahe River, The
original watercourse of Fushe River and many other drainage corridors where bridges and two
grade separations shall be built. Collision prevention shall be provided on the bridges to prevent
vehicles from falling into the water, which guarantees bridge strength.
(2) Lightings and Drive With Caution signs and speed limit signs shall be put up on each section to
minimize night traffic accidents.
(3) Design self-contained surface runoff collection system for bridges and grade separations and
use special ditch to direct surface runoff into 1 Om3 - 20m3 catch basin which can deposit, separate
oil and retain noxious substance to reduce impact of accident contamination on the surface water
during raining days.
(4) Road management authority shall check and inspect vehicles transporting dangerous articles
and those that could not present all required certificates or overloaded ones shall not be allowed to
run on the road.
5.3.3 Emergency Plan
The plan in this project shall be included in the emergency plans of Middle Ring project.
The content in the emergency plan includes responsibilities and tasks of control center and other
cooperative departments, emergency technologies, choice of treatment procedures, arrangement
of equipment and instrument, provide and arrangement of labor and material resources, accident
dynamic monitoring system and accident report system. This plan shall be included in the
emergency plan of entire Middle Ring project.
(1) Set up emergency network, team and superintendent.
Led by Communication Bureau of Wuhan Municipality, Bureau of Environmental Protection of
Wuhan Municipality, Wuhan Environmental Inspection Detachment, Wuhan Environmental
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               94



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN  to PING  ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
Monitoring Center, Bureau of Public Security of Wuhan Municipality, and Wuhan Fire Protection
Group form emergency network. The emergency team which is in charge of accident caused by
dangerous goods transportation is formed by Bureau of Environmental Protection of Wuhan
Municipality, Bureau of Public Security of Wuhan Municipality and Wuhan Fire Protection Group.
Emergency center shall be equipped with telephone and permeant person on duty 24hours. If
accident happens, inform superintend to connect with the team so as to notify relevant units and
locals to organize personnel, vehicles and medicines to treat emergency.

6. Public Participation
Public participation is important for environmental influence assessment of construction project to
communicate construction unit and assessment unit with common people, by which environmental
issue highlighted by the public is indeed understood to assist the related department in
establishing feasible environmental protection measure so that environmental assessment of
construction project is publicized and conclusion is drawn for reality to ensure expected social
economic benefit of construction project is realized.
6.1 Purpose of Public Participation
(1)The public can understand basic information on construction project, influences on road under
or after construction and proposed planning and measure for understanding, support and
cooperation of the public.
(2)The queried result from the local resident can analyze the feature of polluted environment and
current status quality of environmental element to reflect objective degree of environmental
assessment and protect the public's interest.
(3)By means of the public participation the local resident for the project is invited to confirm
environmental protection measure and understand their request to ensure environmental
protection measure recommended in the assessment is feasible and efficient.
(4)Channel is prepared for feasibility of the public participation for the project and decision item.
6.2 Performance of public participation
6.2.1 Investigation scope
Investigation is made for the possibly-influenced area by the project construction in compliance
with environmental assessed area of the proposed road.
6.2.2 Respondent
The respondent refers to directly-influenced resident including the local farmer, worker and
governmental staff, teacher and student etc.
6.2.3 Investigation method
Investigation is made by means of random questionnaire and interview. The investigator
introduces the basic information on proposed project to the respondent in detail, including project
scale, route orientation and positive or negative influence on the local, and then the respondent
fills out the public opinion questionnaire or dictates opinion on his/her will for record, and the
working unit or home addresses, sex, age, ethnicity, education background and status of family
member of respondent are indicated. Finally the environmental assessment unit arranges,
summarizes and analyzes the public participation questionnaire submitted.
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                98



The third ring north seetion (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project enviroanrent influence statement (for app,o-al)
6.2.4 Investigation details
Investigation refers to basic information on the respondent and the followings:
(l)Whether the road construction is approved?
(2)Whether the route selection and orientation of the road are approved?
(3)Whether the traffic status in existed area is satisfactory?
(4)Whether the road construction is beneficial for the local economic development?
(5)Do you approve that partial farmland is used for road construction and some buildings are
removed?
(6)Whether compensation policy of road expropriation/removal is understood?
(7)Whether expropriation/removal and relocation is approved?
(8) Is there requirement for compensation on relocation?
(9)ls there influence of road construction on you?
(0)Which measures to be taken to minimize influence?
(1)Other opinion or suggestion of the public
See the appendix 3 for the sample form of the public participation for investigation.
6.2.5 Information on investigation performance
With the support of construction unit assessment unit first released environmental influence
assessment on the project construction in website http://www.whciwzb.com/info/1095-1.htm of
administration office of foreign investment utilization for urban construction of Wuhan on March 15,
2007. Webpage is shown in the appendix 4.
Construction unit performed the public questionnaire on project route from March 26 to 29, 2007,
during the period of which interview was made for the partial public.
On May 27, 2007 assessment unit released the simplified edition of environmental assessment
report in http://www.whciwzb.com of administration office of foreign investment utilization for urban
construction of Wuhan.
6.3 Public investigation result
6.3.1  Investigation result of questionnaire and interview
(l)Release and return of questionnaire
70 questionnaires are released in total, 63 questionnaires are actually returned and questionnaire
return rate is 90%. All the returned questionnaires are effective.

Statistics is made for the effective returned questionnaire. See Table 6-1 for structure of
respondent.

(3)Result of questionnaire
Assessment team summarizes result of the public random questionnaire. Such result is described
as follows:
(DThe public attitude toward the project construction
The respondents approve the project construction, 68.3% respondents support route selection
and orientation for the project, only 6.3% respondents disapprove route selection and orientation
for the project and 25.4% respondents don't know whether to support route selection and
orientation for the road.
(9)The public attitude toward traffic status of the area
82.5% respondents dissatisfy traffic status of the area.
(2)The public attitude toward expropriation/removal and relocation
53.9% respondents approve partial farmland occupation and housing removal for the project
construction. 41.3% respondent has disputes on such issue and 4.8% respondents are unaware
of it.
The understanding status for compensation policy of highway expropriation/removal shows that
those who have understanding is only 7.9%, those who have a little understanding is 39.7 and
those who have no understanding is only 52.4%.
36.5% respondents approve expropriation/removal and relocation and others approve it with
conditions.
For request for relocation compensation 41.3% respondents claim economic compensation,
66.7% respondents require the nearby relocation and 8% approve economic compensation or
nearby relocation with no request for change in occupation or others.
FA)The public attitude toward influence of the project construction and protection measure
96.8% respondents show that the highway construction project benefits the economic
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection             100



The third ring north section (SAN  JINTAN  to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
development of the area without any disadvantages.
For environmental influence of the highway construction project 55.6% respondents show that the
influence is noise, 31.7% respondents show that it is tail gas and 38.1 % respondent show that it is
dust.
For protection measure on influence 93.7% respondents choose road greening, 6.3% respondents
require sound insulation or village separation and 15.9% shows that there is no other choice.
See Table 6-2 for summarized results of the public random questionnaire.

(4)lnvestigation result
Statistics and analysis for the public investigation result show:
OThe respondent of the project support construction for the proposed project, so the project
construction is supported and approved by common people.
2The respondent can understand environmental influence and relief measures of project
construction, so the common people along the highway is conscious of environmental protection
but not all.
)The most of people have a little understanding for road construction and removal compensation
policy of state and Hubei Province. The public propaganda is not well performed and the partial
public is not enough concerned with his/her benefit; therefore construction unit will take an
initiative in strengthening propaganda of highway construction.
)Most of the respondents require nearby relocation and traffic safety and convenient life for
resident, which shows that the public support the development and construction for the area.
Design unit considers layout of passage and over-bridge and construction for drainage facilities
according to actual situation.
(5)Road construction brings influence on normal living, traffic and production. The respondent will
accept it but construction unit will minimize such influence.
(5)The public participation and suggestion feedback
For the public suggestion and request for road construction assessment team will submit
suggestion feedback to project construction department and make suggestion for construction
department and construction unit.
OConstruction department
Construction department will cooperate with the local government to fully utilize propaganda
method and greatly promote project construction and compensation policy for removal/relocation
and expropriation, protect benefit of the relocated household and obtain the public understanding
and supporting for the project.
The specific, effective and feasible measures on expropriation/removal/relocation are established
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                  102



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
according to the state and local policy and regulation. The related municipal/provincial/state poicy
is executed for the removal and relocation. Compensation on expropriation/removal will be
actually carried out to ensure the benefit of the removed and expropriated household.
Construction unit will receive suggestion from the influenced person, reasonably select route,
minimize occupation of cultivated land, reduce damage for agricultural facilities, rationally arrange
passage and facilitate resident trip.
For road section with over-standard noise the related measures will be taken to minimize the
influence to be acceptable. Scattered household which suffer from over-standard noise may be
removed and relocated.
(®)Construction unit
Construction unit will conclude civilization construction contract at the time of contract conclusion.
For construction of the crossing section of the existed road the transportation is organized in place
to avoid blocking and cutting. The side ditch is excavated well for construction of water source
section of farmland and irrigation to ensure no slurry water for construction flows into farmland
without influence on farmland cultivation.
During the period of construction mechanical noise, construction fly ash and domestic sewage and
rubbish for construction team cause influence on resident life and work. Construction unit will
follow civilization construction to relieve environmental pollution; particularly construction fly ash
has great impact on resident in summer, so construction unit will schedule frequency and quantity
of sprinkling.
Construction unit will prohibit night construction (22: 00-6:00) of high-noise machine; Construction
time will be adjusted for construction of sensitive section. Construction nearby the school will be
planned during the period of vacation. Enclosure and caution sign is arranged at construction site
or temporary measures is taken for noise reduction, including wood sound insulation plate or
semi-underground construction. For consecutive construction hour construction unit will contact
environmental department according to actual situation, apply for night construction permit
certificate and release announcement to strive support.
Construction unit will use low-noise machine and noise measurement will be made for
construction mechanical equipment under the normal operation condition in advance. Access
construction shall not be performed for over-state standard machinery. Equipment will be
maintained in the process of construction to avoid noise enhancement caused by unfavorable
equipment performance.
The project site is area with schistosomicides infection, so construction unit will strengthen
management and construction personnel will take necessary protection measures to avoid
epidemic spread for underwater work.

6.4 Typical Public Opinion and Acceptance
6.4.1 Typical public opinion
In the process of questionnaire all the respondents approve the project execution, but four
persons (accounting for 6.3% of the respondent) disagree route selection and orientation for the
highway, 26 persons (accounting for 41.3% of the respondent) make suggestions on farmland and
housing removal.
Besides investigation, adopting partial public feedback and suggestion, are summarized as follows:
road construction in residential quarter and environmental protection is correlative to life quality
and health, so governmental department shall minimize the disadvantages on environment;
auxiliary road is constructed for the village section, sewage drainage and oil stain works are done
well, farmer living is arranged properly and traffic noise and safety are managed in place; State
construction is foremost and farmer living is highlighted to reflect favorable policy of CPC and
multiple system for farmer's benefit protection.
6.4.2 Acceptance of the public opinion
(l)Disagreement on route selection and orientation of road
Investigated by assessment team, four persons, who disagree route selection, is expropriated
farmer. The relocation compensation plan is not confirmed at the time of investigation and objector
is shortage of understanding for expropriation compensation policy and anxious for influence of
expropriation on living, therefore they disagree orientation. At present the preparation for
relocation and removal plan is completed. The project team makes pre-phase propaganda for
resident. With callback made by assessment team the objector agrees route selection and
orientation.
(2)Opinion on occupied farmland and removed housing
People who approve farmland occupation and housing removal are 41.3% of the respondent.
During the period of investigation investigators absorb the suggestion from the respondent,
through which most of people is shortage of understanding for relocation compensation plan
because the relocation and removal plan for the project is not completed. Analysis on opinionist
questionnaire shows that those who is utterly shortage of understanding for expropriation/removal
compensation policy account for 81.8% of opinionist, those who have a little understanding for it is
19.2% and there is no person who fully understands it.
At present relocation and removal plan for the project is completed. Project team makes
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               104



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
pre-phase propaganda for resident. The resident can understand relocation compensation. For
relocation and removal plan statistics will be made for selection of currency compensation or
physical material distribution according to the removed household will, therefore the assessment
shows that the public approves compensation and relocation specified in the project.
(3)Public opinion and suggestion
For the public opinion and suggestion assessment unit presents feedback to project construction
unit and project design unit. Construction unit will take full consideration for the public opinion and
suggested measures. Project design and enforcement for construction management will be made
to avoid influence of project construction on residential living environment.
For the public focus on noise pollution from the project site noise reduction and sound insulation
will be made for important road section with over-standard noise specified in project design.
Sound insulation barrier and removal will be made for residential quarter and school with
over-standard noise, through which noise value is satisfactory without any influence on residential
living and school education.

7. Environmental management plan and Supervision Plan
Strict scientific environmental management must be established during project construction, under
the supervision of relevant authority; the environmental management plan, environmental
monitoring plan and construction environment supervision on environment protection shall be
executed to ensure effective control and precaution of adverse environmental impact during
Construction and operation period to achieve harmonization of of environment, economic and
social benefits.
7.1 Environmental management
The environment management of construction project may approximately divide into three stages
including early stage, Construction Period and operation period according to the execution time. In
each stage, there is different management body, process and management content for different
structure activities and contents.
7.1.1  Preconstruction Environmental Management
At preconstruction stage of the project, environmental management includes the management
during the period of construction design of next stage and subcontract. The executor of early stage
enviromental management is the Employer----Wuhan urban construction utilization of foreign
investment project management office.
During the construction design stage, the related departments in wuhan directly supervise the
Employer and Designer on executioning the Environment Protections submitted from
"Environmental Impact Report" and formally approved by Wuhan Environmental Protection
Bureau (WHEPB), These environmental measures will be included in the investment budget and
be fully reflected in constuction design to achieve ENVIRONMENTAL PROJECTS "three
simultaneous" requirement.
During construction subcontracting process, Employer shall bring forward the environment
protection request against the construction organization program according to the related
requirements of Environmental Impact Report and the formally reply from Wuhan Environmental
Protection Bureau (WHEPB), and shall give Priority SELECTION to the construction unit with
strong environmental awareness good performance of environmental works and Excellent
capability to lay the foundation for Civilized construction and high quality execution of
environmental protections. The builders shall be given training related with environmental
protection laws and Ecological protection and pollution prevention before access the scene, there
should be laws and regulations on environmental protection and ecological protection, pollution
control and other aspects of training. Construction for environmental management and
environmental requirements of the Commissioner shall work on the project as one of the terms of
contracts. The environmental management requirement and environmental supervision during
construction period shall be considered one of the articles of the construction subcontract.

7.1.2 Environmental management in the period of construction
(1) Management system
During construction period, the executor of environmental management shall be Employer and the
supervisory organ will include Wuhan Environmental Protection Bureau (WHEPB), Wuhan
Environmental Inspection Detachment(WHEID), Jiang'an District Environment Protection
Administration, Huangpi District Environment Protection Administration, construction control unit,
Employer as well as traffic management department, environmental protection department, etc, in
a specific or sensitive terms, banking, auditing, judicial, the news media will also become one of
the supervision bodies, which together constitute a construction period of the environmental
management system.
(2) Management duty
In the management system, to strengthen the construction of its own environmental awareness
and environmental management shall be the first step. Employer shall employ full-time or
part-time staff in charge of construction work on environmental protection and of self-supervision
and management of pollution control measures at construction site such as discharge of
wastewater, dust, Construction noise who shall be trained Engineering Staff possessing the
necessary competence and qualifications and being given relevant responsibility and the right to
adequately perform their forefront duties of environmental protection supervision. Environmental
Management Accountability and environmental protection Assessing System shall be established to
organize the main leadership for training in the knowledge of environmental protection, raise
environmental awareness.
Supervision units shall take the various environmental projects and measures in Environmental
Impact Report, ENVIRONMENTAL PROJECTS construction design documents and construction
contract as a major content of the Supervision work, carry out the strict checks of the
environmental project quality and supervision of the Employer to execution the various
environmental protections, and after the construction, shall submit Environmental Supervision
report. Environmental Supervisor should be entitled during the construction who shall make
detailed Environmental Supervision plan including construction noise control, especially noise
control at night, dust control, and civilized construction and so forth.
During construction The Main Function of the Employer for environmental management shall be to
grasp the overall situation and the full environmental dynamic of construction, actively organize to
resolve the major environmental problems or disputes, and to assist the construction unit to
properly handle the relationship with the environmental departments, and with the public as well
as the Stakeholders
In preparation of construction the Environmental Protection shall mainly include how to protect the
interests of Removed Residents and units in process of removing. Employer shall determine
