(2) Monitoring report system
The monitoring reports during construction and operation periods shall be prepared by Wuhan
Environmental Monitoring Center, 4 times a year at constrution stage and once at operation stage; and
the repeorts will send to contractor in construction and to road management department in operation,
which bath will deliver to Wuhan Municipal Communication Commission and Wuhan Environmental
Protection Bureau (WHEPB). The reports will include the monitoring results and the discussion about
the environmental quality meeting the criterion during the monitoring period, and any exceeding or
unexpected adverse impact was found, the CONTROLS AND PRECAUTIONS shall be designed and
reviewed by the government departments to execution the agreement.
Construction period will be about 1.5 years, and the cost for monitoring is estimated 60,000 yuan;
monitoring costs in operation period will be about 50,000 yuan / year. As Proposed projects into
operation period, Highway Maintenance squad along the line shall be equipped with the full-time staff
for environmental conservation projects, Responsibling for the day-to-day maintenance of the Side
Slope Green, subgrade drainage protection engineering and maintenance, bridges, culverts and other
routine maintenance.

8. Environment economic gain and loss analysis
Generally speaking, in assessing the investment effect on a project the economic benefit, social
benefit and environment benefit are adopted for weighing. Since Environment resources are not
renewable, more and more importance is attached to the loss of social economic benefit and
ecologic benefit of the environment caused by this project; however, there is no mature approach
of quantitative estimate available with regard to the environment economic gain and loss. It is
impossible to calculate direct economic gain of this project, as a part of center ring highway of
Wuhan City once opening to traffic under the policy of no charging around center ring highway.
Therefore, assessment herewith only performs qualitative analysis on social benefit and
Environment economic gain and loss.
8.1 Social benefit analysis
8.1.1  Improving urban and regional traffic conditions
This Project is one section last constructed for the third ring highway. Upon completion the third
ring highway will be run through, and traffic structure in city center will be improved, and traffic
pressure therein will be abated, since the third ring will assume most transit traffic of Wuhan.
As for the area along this project, with the establishment of grade separations on Han-Huang
Highway and Nanhu Village, and passages with both inlet and outlet from the right side on
Jianshequ Road and Xingchen Avenue. The traffic communication within the area will become
closer, thus the traffic capability of such area will be elevated and traffic framework will be
consummated.
8.1.2 Promoting regional land development and utilization
The project will connect Houhu New Town and Huangpu High-tech Town and has created a
favorable condition for connection of two newly-planned towns. Now within the Houhu New Town
and Huangpu High-tech Town lands along the planned line are farmland, upon completion of this
Project with the massive improvement of traffic condition the surrounding land development and
utilization will be promoted and the planning for Houhu New Town and Huangpu High-tech Town
will be put into effect as soon as possible.
8.1.3 Promoting coordinated development of regional economy
The improvement of traffic condition and the development and utilization of lands along the
planned line as scheduled, on one hand, will promote the development of economy of the area
along the planned line, and on the other hand, will drive the development of related industry, thus
a phase of harmonic and benign development of regional economy will be created.
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection              116



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Rond drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
8.2 Environment benefit analysis
8.2.1  Environment loss caused by Project Construction
Lands along the planned line under this project are primarily used for farming vegetables and
aquiculture; secondarily for urban construction, i.e. housing and utilities such as irrigation and
drainage ditch, river course and drainage corridor and so on. The Environment loss caused by
project construction is demonstrated on:
(1) The loss of biomass arising from land occupation, including agricultural vegetation, aquatic
product, wilding and a small quantity of wild animals.
(2) The pollution caused by running vehicles, including tail gas pollution and noise pollution.
(3) The roadway is constructed in the format of embankment where there are trestles and bridges
with appropriate distance, although there are transit facilities such as passages and pipe culverts,
as a whole ground separation will be formed, which will impact the inhabitation of animals on
ground and thus cause reduction of wild animals within the area along the section.
8.2.2 Environment benefit of Project Construction
The Project will be one part of the third ring highway line, a regional traffic work, construction of
which will have remarkable social benefit. During Project Construction and Operation, appropriate
environment benefit will be produced.
(1) The forestation on trunk road will increase biomass, including plantation of all vegetables, trees
and swards.
(2) Upon completion, such project, serving as a part of entire third ring line, will assume the most
transit traffic in north part of Wuhan (north bank of Changjiang River), relieve traffic pressure of city
center, thus traffic pressure in city center is abated. In addition, vehicles' tail gas contamination
concentrated in city center will be dispersed. The analysis shall be based on that the same volume
of traffic will discharge equivalent volume of contamination. Discharge concentrated on one road is
obviously much more liable to form air pollution that discharge dispersed on one more roads. From
this point execution of this project is benefit for relieving vehicles' tail gas contamination or
formation of pollution.
(3) During project execution, in order to protect acoustic Environment quality along the planned line,
such actions as acoustic shield and relocation have been taken. On one hand biomass loss
caused during construction can be remedied, on the other hand, actions of noise reduction are
taken to control the extent and area of noise pollution, thus acoustic environment pollution arising
from project operation can be abated.
8.2.3 Brief Analysis on Environment Gain and Loss
It is known from abovementioned analysis that upon completion with all actions taken during
construction phase and operation phase on one hand biomass loss caused during construction
can be remedied; on the other hand acoustic environment pollution arising from project operation
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               117



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
can be abated. With regard to regional air pollution, seen from the result of analysis by analogy,
the air environment quality along the planned line can still be up to corresponding standard.
However, air environment quality in city center is sure to be improved.
To sum up, even though economic benefit is uncalculated in a direct way, this project has
favorable social benefit and good environment benefit, and in accordance with the principle of
synchronized growth of "Environment benefit, social benefit and economic benefit".

The third ring north section (SAN  JINTAN  to PING  ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
9. Conclusion on Assessment
9.1 Project Profile
9.1.1  Brief Introduction
The north ring section of Third Ring Line (Sanjintan - Ping'anpu) is a part of Wuhan Third Ring
Line, passing through Jiang'an District and Huangpi District under Wuhan City. It is expected to be
an urban express road as planned with designed traveling speed of 80km/h, and boundary lines
width of 50m. such section is starting from Sanjintan Grade Separation, crossing down through
Beijing-Guangzhou Railway, turning southward between Guanggan Village and Zhangjiadun
Village, and connecting Ping'anpu Grade Separation around Ping'anpu. The road section is
8243.3m long in total.
Total investment on construction is RMB 0.544 billion (excluding expenses for land requisition and
relocation), of which investment on roadwork is RMB 0.538 billion, and on drainage work RMB
0.006 billion.
The main works are Grade Separation of Han-Huang Highway, Grade Separation of Nanhu
Village, Bridge on Huangxiaohe River, and Bridge on Zhujiahe River, Bridge on Sheshui River Old
Way and flyovers and street-crossing pipe culverts along the section planned.
There is no road in existence along the whole line, while new permanent land occupation will be
886.45 mu, including 350.77mu plow land, 222.51 mu Construction land utilization, and 313.28 mu
water surface. There is basic farmland. It is required to relocate 399 enterprises and households,
totaling 1297 people are to be relocated, and 54877m2 housing is to be relocated.
9.1.2 Comparison and selection routing program
During design comparison and selection on Daijiashan Section and Chenjiaji Section are
performed in a respective way. There are two programs for Daijiashan Section and three for
Chenjiaji Section.
Comparison and selection are also done from the view of Environment Protection against
proposed design program. Through comparison, under assessment we hereby agree on adopting
engineering designer's proposal as recommendation to conduct assessment.
9.2 Construction Time Sequence and Scheduling
9.2.1 Construction Time Sequence
(1) Link with comprehensive improvement work on exit section of Fuhe River
According to schedule of comprehensive improvement work on exit section of Fuhe River, total
time limit for construction is three years. The construction has commenced in November 2005, and
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection             119



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN  to PING  ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence Otatrment (for approval)
is expected to complete in October 2008.
The construction of north section of Third Ring Line will commence in August 2007, and is
expected to complete in October 2008. The commenced date falls behind comprehensive
improvement work on exit section of Fuhe River, while both are expected to complete in
synchronized manner. Therefore, earthwork necessary for construction and waste backfilling can
be linked with such improvement work so as to reduce land occupation and relieve impact on
ecological environment.
(2) Time Sequence Arrangement for this Construction
According to "Huangpu New Town Spatial Plan Layout", Construction of new riverbank and
rebuilding of Zhujiahe River facility are premise and guarantee for construction and development
of Huangpu New Town and corresponding urban infrastructure; in order to prevent Huangpu New
Town and Third Ring Line from being threatened by the flood, Construction of new riverbank and
improvement of Zhujiahe River shall be completed on initial stage. In addition, in order to meet the
need of construction and consider the natural sedimentation of road groundwork sub-grade filling
shall be performed on initial stage.
Prior to completion of new riverbank construction for Fuhe River, first of all Section from Sanjintan
to Han-Huang Highway (approximately 1.64km) shall be constructed as planned. Once such
section is open to traffic, Section from Han-Huang Highway to Ping'anpu can be considered of
outgoing from Han-Huang Highway (inner side of Zhanggong Bank), connecting and rebuilding
Dijiao Road and Han-Shi Expressway (widen vehicle lane to 16-22m), and linking Ping'anpu
Grade Separation, so as to have Third Ring Line fulfill regional traffic function as early as possible,
substitute routing of such section is approximately 7.3km long. However, substitute line shall never
be used as an express road, in addition, traffic control is necessary.
Upon completion of new riverbank construction on Fuhe River, construction of north section of
Third Ring Line from Han-Huang River Grade Separation to Ping'anpu.
9.2.2 Construction Scheduling
Preconstruction commenced in January 2007, Construction Period will be from August 2007 to
October 2008, and completion will be in December 2008.
9.3 Environment quality Status
9.3.1 Air Environment Quality
The analysis is performed by using 2005' regular monitoring result of Huaqiao Monitoring Station
in Jiang'an District, and assessment is done by means of single factor quality index. As assessed
according to GB3095-1996 Environment Air Quality Standard Class II Standard, Environment air
annual average single quality index of PM10 in Environment air around project location is above 1,
that is beyond standard; Annual average single quality indexes of both SO2 and NO2 are below 1,
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection              120



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
that is up to standard.
9.3.2 Surface water environment quality status
The receiving body of wastewater is Fuhe River(Huanghualao - section entry to Changjiang River),
and analysis is performed by using 2005' regular monitoring result on Fuhe River, and assessment
shall be performed by means of Standard Index Method. As assessed according to GB3838-2002
Surface Water Environment Quality Standard on Catalog V Water Area, Standard index of total
nitrogen and ammonia nitrogen in Fuhe Riverin 2005 (Huanghua waterlogging - section entry to
Changjiang River) is above 1, that is beyond standard; Standard index of PH, permanganate index,
COD, BOD, total phosphorus, volatile phenol, and petroleum is lower than 1, that is up to standard;
No standard index is calculated for resolved oxygen since temperature remains unmeasured.
9.3.3 Acoustic environment quality status
Monitoring shall be done in accordance with GB/T 3222-94 Acoustic Environment Noise
Measuring Method and GB/T 14623-93 Urban Regional Environment Noise Measuring Method,
and monitoring stations are set on totaling 7 noise-sensitive spots, monitored resulted is assessed
by comparison with Standard. As assessed according to GB3096-93 Urban Regional Environment
Noise Standard Catalog 2 Standard, both nighttime and daytime acoustic level on all monitoring
stations along the planned line are up to standard. That is to say acoustic environment quality
along the planned line is good.
9.4 Environment Impact Predictive Analysis
9.4.1 Construction Period Environment Impact Predictive Analysis
(1) Ecologic Environment Impact Analysis
During Construction Period vegetation and Ecologic Environment will be destructed and biology
diversity of community there will decline; and quantity of amphibian will slightly reduce, around
construction site and areas nearby reptile and animalcule will move away, and population density
of fish around construction area will decline, while construction impact on variety and quantity of
fish there is appropriate; during Construction Period as well as formation stage of borrow pit,
waste pit and sub-grade, due to nudity of soil layer soil erosion is liable to occur in case of raining.
(2)Environment air
(O Dust emission from construction
During Construction Period dusting pollution will occur on concrete mixing station and materials
handling process. Analysis has shown that fly-ash pollution arising from concrete mixing and
dusting pollution caused by construction vehicles shall never be ignored, instead, corresponding
measures shall be taken to abate pollution impact.
(9) Bitumen pollution
Bitumen pollution is arisen out of hot oil evaporation during pavement work. Evaporated bitumen
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               121



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
will impact surrounding air environment to a certain extent. Extent of Impact will be approximately
60m; population on Impact-sensitive spots is much smaller. The Impact-sensitive spots are
Daishan Village, Nahu Village (Group 20), Nahu Village (Xiaohekou Sub-village) and Shuangqiao
Village which is located to a 40m extent from both sides of boundary line; since mechanical
operation is adopted during bitumen paving, and thus operation speed is very high, impact on
such spots is temporary.
(3) Surface water environment
Impact Surface water environment is from household wastewater during Construction Period and
slurry water produced from construction process.
Household wastewater during Construction Period shall be treated in septic tank and then used as
fertilizer, so Impact on Environment is much less.
Most production wastewater during Construction Period is from construction of piers and columns
for bridges and grade separations. Bridge pile foundation construction by means of cofferdam will
lead to enlarging of SS in partial water area, with an impact extent approximately 100m. Slurry for
borehole cast-in-place concrete pile on land shall be recycled, which will have no impact on
environment.
(4) Acoustic Environment
The prediction and calculation on noise of main construction machines have shown that noise
produced by single unit on daytime can conform to standard limit only if maximum distance from
noise source is above 30m; while on nighttime for conforming to standard limit maximum distance
from noise source is above 300m. if one more construction machines are working simultaneously,
the noise produced can conform to Standard Limit only 40m away from the source, while on
nighttime only approximately 350m away from the source, Standard Limit can be met. Time limit
for night construction of construction machines will abate impact on sensitive spots.
(5) Solid wastes
During Construction Period Solid wastes come from earthwork handled, refuse from dismantling of
buildings and household rubbish.
Earthwork to be forwarded outside is approximately 30347m3; transport distance is required to be
within a 5km extent. Since the comprehensive improvement work on exit section of Fuhe Riverwith
construction area is under construction, surplus earthwork from such work (surplus earthwork is
approximately 827645m3, most of which are stacked on inner side of north bank in Chenjiaji) can
be available for construction of this Project, so abovementioned outward earthwork can be
forwarded back to waste pit of comprehensive improvement work on exit section of Fuhe River.
The refuse from dismantling buildings is approximately 279Cm3, all of which is used for sub-grade
and side slope protection.
Since solid wastes are distributed in linearity along the road, inappropriate stacking or disposal will
obstruct agriculture production along the section, and dusting arising from which will impact
inhabitations living around, leading to the increase infectious disease incidence and potential
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               122



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN  to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
infection. So during Construction Period, all wastes shall be cleared away and disposed
immediately so as to reduce and avoid such impact.
(6) Impact from land acquisition and relocation
Construction will occupy permanent land totaling 886.45mu, relocate housing totaling 54877m2.
Occupied farmland will lose farming function forever so living of household depending on occupied
farmland will be impacted in a direct way. Relocation will have a grave impact on the inhibitors'
living area, life quality, habits and even their social relationship, so reasonable compensation and
allocation are necessary.

(2) Analysis on ecologic environment impact
The Impact on terrestrial animal is represented by obstruction impact and environment pollution
impact on animals; all farmland vegetations on permanent land occupied will be destructed.
Traffic noise and illumination of running vehicles during Operation Period and increase of human
activities along road lines will impact normal inhabitation environment of fish and some bottom
fauna in waters nearby to a certain extent. The construction will expel them and cause reduction of
their quantities. However, since only a small area of water surfaces are involved in such project,
any impact on hydrobios will be minor, instead of leading to disappearance of fishes and bottom
fauna in assessed area.
Upon completion, vehicle lanes will be paved with bitumen and imperious, landscaping or slope
protection and side ditch are arranged from curb to boundary line, there is less bare area. So soil
erosion is controlled in an effective way.

(3) Environment air
An analog analysis by adopting actual monitored results for consecutive five days at one go on

Analysis on surface water flow, concentration of contamination in rainwater drained by grade

9.5 Pollution Control and Abatement
9.5.1   Pollution Control and Abatement during Construction Period
(1) Civilized construction control
During Construction Period inappropriate control and unavailability of control measures will be
liable to causing serious pollution to a large extent, impacting people's health, living environment
quality and surrounding environment quality. So Constructor shall fully perform Wuhan Civilized
Construction Administration Procedure and conduct civilized construction, on one hand, to
maintain Wuhan municipal landscape and image, on the other hand, to reduce pollution intensity
during Construction Period, and relieve pollution on sensitive community's living environment.
Civilized construction shall involve enclosure of construction site, material stacking and handling,
temporary facilities, safety facilities, construction noise control, dregs disposal, wastewater
discharge, construction site environment control and so on.
(2) Ecologic environment protection and recovery measures
As for terrestrial animals and plants and hydrobios, appropriate actions and measures shall be
proposed and taken from aspects of ecologic impact avoidance, abatement, recovery and
compensation, and effective control.
Terrestrial plants:
The topsoil on permanent land occupied, temporary land occupied during Construction, waste site,
construction camp shall be peeled off by 30cm, obstruction, setting drain ditch and plant protection
measures shall be taken to avoid soil erosion; upon completion of construction such sites shall be
cleaned and scarified, cultivated soil shall be covered, second plough shall be done, and locally
suitable plants shall be selected for recovery and landscaping on time. Temporary land occupied
for construction shall be allocated in a collective way. Everything shall be placed in good order,
instead of being scattered everywhere; DO NOT left or throw wastes away at random and DO
NOT collapse crops.
It is highly recommended for road landscaping that recovered vegetation area shall never be lower
than original area. During vegetation recovery compensation, in addition to locally adaptable
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                127



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road drainage project environme.t influence statement (for approval)
speeded-up species, staggered distribution of multiple species shall be considered in terms of
plantation layout, so as to improve diversity of plant specifies along road lines, enhance their
disease and vermin resistance as well as stability of gallery. In addition, selected germ chit must
be quarantined to avoid introduction of disease and vermin.
The vegetation recovery with land use extent for highway shall never destruct or minimize any
destruction on vegetation outside road construction boundary. For vegetation recover on both
sides of highway, sub-grade protection and landscaping and environmental protection effect (such
as noise reduction and air pollution) shall be fully considered; and safe traveling (DO NOT screen
drivers' slight line) shall be maintained to ensure normal drive of vehicles.
For protection of embankment, road cut and side slope, local perennial greensward of drought
enduring with root system flourishing, liability to survival, fast growth and good function of
consolidating soil shall be selected. Tree and grass seeds selected shall be adaptable to local
landform, soil and weather. Varieties of choiceness shall be introduced to ensure survival rate of
trees planted.
During both Construction Period and Operation Period ecologic impact shall be monitored and
investigated. The ecological control shall be strengthened through monitoring. For ecologic control
ecologic environment control staff as well as all managerial and reporting regulations shall be
established to conduct environment education within project-impacted area, improve environment
consciousness of construction and managerial personnel. The dynamic monitoring and perfect
management are adopted to make ecologic environment develop toward benign or benefit
direction.
Terrestrial animals:
Improve protection consciousness of construction personnel, and prohibit hunting wild animals.
Investigate construction period and manner, and avoid noise disturbing wild animals. During
Construction Period strengthen protection on borrow site, soil waste site and slag waste site,
enhance management on construction personnel, DO NOT discharge household wastewater to
waters nearby directly so as to abate waters pollution and impact on living environment of animals.
Upon completion make every effort to recover ecologic environment, and minimize adverse impact
on animal caused by destruction of ecologic environment.
Establish an enclosed green belt on bridge location, avoid adverse impact of light and noise on
animals, expedite recovery of vegetation and natural landscaping under bridges, and benefit
animals' adapting to new environment.
Hydrobios:
Prior to such project development and construction, do a good job of preconstruction planning;
during Construction Period strengthen protection on slag waste site and protection on water
environment, avoid pollution on partial water areas along road line and minimize impact on
environment of hydrobios. And do a good job of recovery of ecologic environment upon
completion of construction, and minimize adverse impact on water quality and hydrobios.
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               128



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN  to PING  ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
(3) Air pollution control measures
(o The road sections on such environment-sensitive spots as towns and rural residential area
where construction materials pass by shall be cleaned and watered on a regular basis so as to
reduce secondary dusting, in addition, all contracted construction sections are required to equip at
least one sprinkling cars (purchased or rented); generally do watering once every morning (7:30-
8:30), every noon (12:00-13:00), every evening (17:00-18:00), when wind speed is higher than
3, under a fine weather in summer, do watering every 2 hours.
(9) The measures like paulin coverage and wetting shall be taken for bulk materials truck so as to
reduce dusting pollution to atmosphere, stacked materials shall also be covered with paulin, and
driving routing of trucks shall be kept away from residential areas and environment-sensitive
spots.
( The storage yard and concrete mixing station established for road construction shall be kept far
away from residential areas or other people-crowded areas, but arranged on a clear and empty
place. Storage yard and concrete mixing station shall be located leeward 300m from main
residential areas along the section to reduce pollution impact on inhibitors.
(4) Wastewater pollution abatement during Construction Period
(O Managerial Measures
Perform education concerning water environmental protection on construction sites and camps,
have construction personnel understand the importance of water environment protection;
especially during construction of canal bridge understructure, manage to have the work done in
low water season; in addition, strengthen on construction control and supervision, check
construction machines on a regular basis, and avoid oil leakage and contaminating waters. DO
NOT stack bitumen, oil, chemicals and so on near surface waters, and provide temporary canvas
for sheltering; Take necessary actions to avoid mud and bulk materials blocking water channel or
irrigation ditch and water pipes in existence.
®) Construction slurry and other solid wastes treatment
Manage to reduce wastewater produced from sub-grade and bridgework directly flowing to river
and irrigation channel, reduce ascending of concentration of suspended matters in waters;
process slurry for pile foundation, and then forward slurry produced from the processes of sunk
shaft's suctioning slurry and sinking, water surface pile-drilling and land construction to the site
designated by Constructor for disposal. The selection of slurry disposal site shall be approved by
local authorities. Silts from excavation of pier foundation shall be forwarded to the site designated
on the bank for stacking, instead of being thrown away at random. It is highly recommended to use
borrow site nearby as waste site. The household rubbish shall be collected and then moved away
by municipal and environmental sanitation authorities.
(®) Household wastewater treatment measures during Construction Period
The household wastewater drained from construction camp will impact water environment, such
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               129



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN  to PING  ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
impact on waters will be related to number ot construction personnel. Since there is no municipal
piping network available along the section and locally supporting wastewater treatment plant is not
put into operation, no wastewater from construction is allowed to be drained into natural the
receiving body in a direct way; The construction camp for road section spanning waters shall be
kept away from boundary of waters, and all household wastewaters shall be collected via cesspool
prior to discharge. In consideration that most lands along the section are used for agriculture
purpose, wastewater in cesspool shall be used as fertilizer on farmland.
( Treatment of wastewater and oily water from concrete mixing
A small quantity of alkali wastewater containing SS will be produced from concrete mixing process,
so on concrete mixing yard a sedimentation tank (3x5x2m considerable) shall be established to
collect and treat wastewater. During construction of bored pile slurry produced shall be recycled by
constructing sedimentation tank and ditch.
(5) Noise pollution control during Construction Period
© Try to use low-noise machines. The construction machines shall be serviced on a regular basis
during construction, and noise shall be enhanced due to poor operation of construction machines.
© NO high-noise machine working on nighttime ( 22:00-6:00 next day).
( According to Noise Limit on Construction Yard, appropriate construction boundary dimension
shall be determined to avoid setting construction camp near villages.
( Scheduling handling of construction materials in an appropriate way: The trucks shall slowdown
and keep silent when passing through villages and towns as well as schools.
(6) Abatement of impact from land requisition and relocation
The Constructors shall focus their attention to impact from land requisition and relocation on
residing people along the section. According to World Bank OP4.12 Policies and national and
Hubei Provincial Policies on resettling and relocation, a relocation initiative plan has been made to
detailing reasonable compensation to land occupation and relocation, resettlement of impacted
people and special organization established for such work, ensuring execution of all regulations on
land requisition and relocation, striving for minimizing Construction Impact on people along the
section and making every effort to ensure living quality of impacted people shall not decline due to
such Construction but increase and letting impacted people benefit from such Construction.
The estimated expense for compensation is approximately RMB 253.363 million; as for people
who request physical resettlement, resettling offices shall consult pertinent district governmental
authorities and street government, and convene villagers' representative meeting for discussion to
select proper location for house sites for settlement in vicinity. The impacted villagers shall be
allocated house sites of 80-1OOm2 per household. Expenses for road access, power supply and
water supply facility connection and site clearance shall be covered by Project Office.
In addition, five impacted businesses and four impacted households from depressed communities
are covered. The impacted businesses shall be compensated in cash and allowed to establish and
run their own stores before dismantling and upon completion of construction; depressed
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               130



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPIJ) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
communities shall be compensated in cash.
9.5.2 Pollution control and abatement during Operation Period
(1) Air pollution control and abatement
Since such project belongs to urban public traffic facility and will be opened to all vehicles
acceptable, vehicles' tail gas pollution control shall mainly depend on governmental
micro-instruction, in addition, highway administration shall control vehicles running on the road in a
practical way. The actions for abatement of air pollution: (0 continue to take measures of
controlling discharge and pollution of vehicles in existence. (9) implement vehicles' discharge and
pollution control strategy. (M) adopt appropriate measures to control vehicles' discharge and
pollution. For example: foresting and landscaping can be performed on vacant lands and humps
within the controlled extent, trees selected will be able to absorb contaminations discharged by
vehicles. It is also necessary to control vehicles running on the road, not to allow vehicles under
poor condition or overloading access to highway, but maintain the highway on time, keep the road
smooth, and avoid increase of contamination discharge caused by vehicles' abnormal driving.
(2) Noise control measurement
During Operation Period, in order to keep good acoustic environment quality on both sides of
highway, a series of measures such as highway noise reduction per se, engineering control and
planning control specifications along highway line.
(0) Noise reduction measurement
This assessment proposes to establish sound insulated screens on single side or double sides of
the sections around sensitive spots, resettle inhibitors living within a 30m extent from the boundary
line, reserve expenses for future environment relocation, additional investment for noise pollution
control will total RMB 22.73 million, and RMB 14 million shall be reserved for future resettling and
relocating of inhibitors living within 50m or 150m extent on both sides of road from the boundary
line on both sides of road.
() Engineering management measurement
Strengthening highway traffic control such as restricting vehicles of poor performance entering into
highway and setting markings of speed governed or whistle prohibited on both ends of sections
around key sensitive spots can control noise pollution in an effective way. The highway shall be
maintained on a regular basis to maintain smoothness of pavement and to avoid increase of traffic
noise caused by vehicles' failure in normal driving.
) Planning control specifications
The houses rebuilt by inhibitors along the section shall be kept far away from Third Ring Line;
planning of housing areas shall refer to the schedule of noise prediction scope on both road sides
under this report and a certain distance (generally 200m from road centerline) for protection shall
be determined in combination with local landform condition and be kept away from the highway, in
addition, the inhibitors along the section shall build their new houses beyond appropriate
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection                131



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPU) Road dr-inage project environment influence statement (for nppro-nI)
protection interval, otherwise, they shall be responsible for any traffic noise impact caused to
them.
The sensitive spots such schools, hospitals, clinics and rest homes demanding high acoustic
environment requirement shall be located 250m away from the road. It is inappropriate to
construct these buildings within 250m extent of the boundary line.
9.5.3 Countermeasure and actions for reduction of risk
Handling of hazardous substances must be controlled according to Regulation on Transport of
Hazardous Substances (TT3130). In order to safeguard handling of hazardous substances, it is
required to do a good job of risk analysis, master nature and change law of risk, well protect
packing, transport, handling, storage and custody of hazardous substances. All consignment
formalities and documentation shall be procured according to relevant laws and regulations.
Control measures and precautions shall be taken against all environmental conditions during
transport, and an appropriate emergency solution shall be formulated. Practice has demonstrated
all hazardous substances can be transported in a safe manner if abovementioned procedures are
handled.
9.6 Public Participation
The survey on public along the section who are under the direct impact is performed in forms of
questionnaire and interview, and publicized on htto://www.whciwzb.com.
9.6.1 Result of questionnaire survey
The assessing group has collected all results of questionnaire survey on public by random
sampling. The survey results are described as follows:
(D Public attitude toward such Project Construction
All informants have expressed their consent on such Project Construction, and 68.3% of them
support road line selection and routing direction, only 6.3% disagree on road line selection and
routing direction, and another 25.4% have no idea on whether to support such road line selection
and routing direction.
(X Public attitude toward local traffic condition
82.5% of all informants have shown they are unsatisfactory to local traffic condition.
® Public attitude toward land requisition/relocation
For partial field and relocated housing to be occupied for such project construction, 53.9% of all
informants have expressed no objection, 41.3% have expressed their objection, and only 4.8%
have no idea toward such issues.
For knowledge on policy of land requisition/relocation compensation for highway construction only
7.9% show their knowledge on such policy, 39.7% know some and 52.4% show no knowledge.
For whether to obey land requisition/move and relocation, 36.5% informants show their obedience
and others show conditional obedience.
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               132



The third ring north sectiot (SAN JINTAN  to PING  ANPU) Road drainage project ervironment influence statement (for approval)
For requirement on compensation for relocation, 41.3% informants require economic
compensation, 66.7% require settlement in vicinity, and including 8% require either economic
compensation or settlement in vicinity. And no informant requires changing jobs or anything else.
) Public attitude toward Impact caused by such Project Construction and due precautions to be
taken
96.8% informants deem that such Road Construction will benefit local economic development and
that no disadvantage is found.
For Environment Impact caused by such Road Construction, 55.6% informants deem that noise is
a key impacting factor, 31.7% deem that vehicles' tail gas is a key factor; and 38.1% consider
dust.
For precautions against such impact, 93.7% informants first select road landscaping, 6.3% require
setting acoustic shield and 15.9% require being far away from villages and towns. And nobody has
selected other issues.
9.6.2  Typical public opinions
According to our questionnaire all respondents agree on execution of this project, four (accounting
for 6.3% of total number of respondents) of them disagree on the routing and direction of such
road, 26 respondents (accounting for 41.3%) have objection to partial land occupation and
housing relocation.
In addition, during our survey detailed feedback and suggestions have been acquired, excerpts of
which are detailed as follows: since the road construction will pass through residential area,
environmental protection involves inhibitors' living quality and health. The governmental
authorities are expected to minimize adverse factors of Impact Environment; an access road is
required to pave a road in our village, provide favorable blow-down and drainage works, do a good
job of resettling farmers, and take measures against traffic noise and traffic safety; so importance
shall be attached to both national economic construction and villagers' life, and good policies of
CPC and a multiple system safeguarding villagers' interest shall be demonstrated.
9.6.3 Adoption of Public Opinions
(1) Objection to road routing and direction
The survey made by Assessing Group shows that abovementioned four persons disagree on road
routing because their farmlands are to be occupied. Since during survey resettlement
compensation program remains undetermined, the objectors have no idea on polices of land
requisition and compensation, they are afraid that their life will be impacted, so they choose to
object road routing. Now related relocation and resettlement program has been developed, Project
Staff has made such program known to inhibitors along the section. Return visit by our assessing
group shows that such objectors now agree on the routing and direction.
(2) Objection on occupation of farmland and relocation of housing
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection               133



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN  to PING  ANPU) Road drainage project environment influence statemsent (for approval)
The public who object occupation of farmland and relocation of housing accounts for 41.3% of all
informants. During our survey, we listen attentively to opinions of all informants; most objectors
said that they were not clear to Project Resettlement and Compensation Program. This is because
such resettlement and relocation plan remains uncompleted. Analysis on objectors' questionnaires
shows that 81.8% objectors have no knowledge on land requisition and resettlement policies, and
only 19.2% know a little, and nobody know.
Now such program has been developed and Project Staff has given initial publicity to inhibitors
along the section. The public along the section has a little knowledge toward resettlement and
compensation. In such program statistic on cash compensation and practicality resettlement have
been made according to the willing of who are resettled. So according to our assessment public
along the section has accepted such program.
(3) Specific public opinion and suggestions
Assessors have feedback specific public suggestions and opinions to Constructors and Designers.
Constructors commit themselves to fully consider public opinions and suggestions, and avoid any
environment impact on inhibitors around from construction by taking actions of engineering design
and construction control.
Whereas public opinions focus on noise pollution around project location, Designers propose to
take noise reduction and sound insulation actions on critical sections where noises exceed
standard. With regard to impacted residential areas and schools where noises exceed standard,
such actions like sound insulated screen and relocation are taken to keep noise level conformable
and minimize impact on inhibitors' life and schools' education.
9.7 Planning conformity analysis
This Project is a component of north section of Wuhan Third Ring Line, starting from Sanjintan and
ending at Ping'anpu. Analysis has shown that Project Construction conform to Wuhan Municipal
Overall Planning and Wuhan's Eleventh Five-Year Plan.
9.8 Conclusion on Environment Feasibility
This Project is a component of Wuhan Third Ring Line, Construction of which will be of great
significance for improving traffic condition of Houhu New Town and Huangpu High-tech New Town
and even Wuhan City center, and comply with Wuhan Urban Overall Planning. The result of public
participation has indicated that local people understand necessity of Construction and support
such Construction.
The Proposed work, during both Construction Period and Operation Period will have impact of
different degrees on acoustic environment, environment air and surface water environment of
assessed area. Major impact shall be Construction Period impact and traffic noise impact during
Operation Period. With control measures taken, Environment Impact can be minimized. With
proper actions on construction scheduling, civilized construction, and noise reduction, neither
Wuhan Municipal Research Institute of Environmental Protection              134



The third ring north section (SAN JINTAN to PING ANPIU) Road drainage project environment influence statement (for approval)
Project Construction nor Operation will impact normal life of inhibitors on sensitive spots. The
analysis on Environment economic gain or loss has shown that Construction will have obvious
social benefit and better Environment benefit. During project bidding process, Environment
Protection during Construction Period shall be specified in bidding documentation and related
contracts. The Constructor shall be responsible for executing environmental protection.
To sum up, Project Construction is feasible from view of Environment Protection.
